Prior: **GR.5 ‚Äî activity monitor** [plan `plans/2026-07-17-guardrails.md` Task 5, **$0**, server-only, no schema/migration/CSS/extension change]: new pure `src/x/monitor.ts` + `GET /x/monitor` (`src/x/routes/monitor.ts`, always mounted, static path) + MCP `x_monitor` (**20 tools now**). Five rules over MY OWN actions ‚Äî `postBurst` (>4 originals/24h, or two under 20 min apart), `replyBurst` (>10 pasted replies in the densest hour of a 3 h lookback ‚Üí warn, >15 ‚Üí critical), `nearDuplicate` (3-word-shingle Jaccard ‚â•0.8 between originals in 14 d), `unfollowChurn` (‚â•25 marks/24h ‚Üí warn, ‚â•`DAILY_CEILING` 40 ‚Üí critical, both constant and window **imported from `connections.ts`** so the alert can only fire when the queue is out-run by hand), `scheduleCluster` (pending slots <45 min apart ‚Üí info). **At most ONE alert per rule** (`postBurst`'s two sub-conditions fold into one message), sorted severity-desc; `{alerts, worst, checkedAt}`. ¬ß7.19 gates deliberately do NOT apply ‚Äî a count of my own actions is not an inference about an audience. Thread tails are self-replies, so `is_reply = false` keeps a 6-tweet thread out of the burst rule for free. `loadMonitorInputs(now)` is exported for GR.6's brief block (one owner of the windows) ‚Äî **GR.6 consumes it; `shingleJaccard` and the thresholds are likewise imported by the calendar's advisory.** Prior: **GR.4 ‚Äî People-tab Following subtab** [plan `plans/2026-07-17-guardrails.md` Task 4, **$0**, extension-only, no server/schema/migration/route/test change]: `PeoplePanel` opens with a `SubTabs` **Roster | Following** switch (the dossier view is outside it ‚Äî a click-through from either subtab still lands on the same `DossierView`). The Following view is the curation surface: a freshness banner (`.warn` when `lastCompleteRunAt` is null or >7 d ‚Äî "run a Following harvest"), a window/daily budget line, the released batch (profile anchor ‚Üí x.com, `file` ‚Üí dossier, `unfollowed ‚úì` ‚Üí `PATCH {status:'done'}`, `keep` ‚Üí `PATCH {keep:true}`), and a collapsed **Ledger** `Section` (search + status filter over `GET /x/following`, two-way keep toggle ‚Äî the only way back from a pin). **Every load of the queue is a write** (`GET /following/queue` releases rows read-time), which is why the view reloads after each PATCH instead of mutating locally, and why the two empty states are distinguished by `eligibleTotal` (>0 with an empty batch = cap reached, not "nobody left"). Prior: **CA.1 + CA.2 step 1 ‚Äî cost-audit follow-ups** [URGENT jump, plan `plans/2026-07-23-cost-audit-followups.md`, **$0**, server-only, no migration/route/extension change, two commits]: **CA.1** ‚Äî `pullMentions` incremental pulls (live `since_id`) now page to X's 800 hard cap (`MENTIONS_HARD_CAP` in `mentions.ts`) via `getUserMentions`'s new `maxTotal` option ‚Äî a TOTAL ceiling across pages; the per-request `max_results` clamp is untouched (invariant #5 ‚Äî completeness comes from more pages under the boundary, never a wider request). Kills the silent inbox data loss (prod returned exactly 50 rows/day since Jul 14 while inbound ran 50‚Äì90; the tail fell below the next pull's checkpoint permanently). A caller-supplied `maxResults` stays a TOTAL cap (the route's ‚â§200 and smoke `--live` ‚â§10 promises hold); a cold pull (no checkpoint) keeps the bounded 50. New `src/x/mentions.test.ts` (+4, suite 1224‚Üí**1228**) stubs `globalThis.fetch` with multi-page fixtures at 9.2e18-prefixed ids. **CA.2 step 1 (instrument-only, NO cost_usd change)** ‚Äî `xFetch` now logs `[cost-audit] <method> <endpoint>: data=N includes.tweets=N includes.users=N` on any 2xx X read whose body carries `includes`: the `expansions` param drags every reply's parent tweet (someone else's post) into `includes.tweets`, which `itemCount` never counted ‚Äî the suspected mechanism behind the console-vs-`/cost/today` divergence (~90 hidden objects/day at 90 replies/day since Jul 17). After a real 03:00 pass, grep the journal for `[cost-audit]`, write the confirm/refute one-liner into PHASE-HISTORY, and only if confirmed do step 2 (preferred: drop `referenced_tweets.id` from the metrics-read expansions ‚Äî `in_reply_to_tweet_id` survives on the tweet's own `referenced_tweets` FIELD; fallback: bill `data.length + includes.tweets.length`). Prior state, still current: **GR.3 ‚Äî following curation queue** [xhigh, dep GR.1‚úì, **$0**, server-only] closes the last gate before the People-tab Following subtab: new pure `src/x/connections.ts` (7-day grace, 6h/15‚Äì18-per-window jittered cap, 40/day ceiling ‚Äî all opening guesses) + `GET /following/queue` registered ABOVE `/following/:handle` (¬ß7.20). All read-time (¬ß7.12): the whitelist (people mutual/ally + `loadTargetHandles()`), eligibility, and the cadence budget are recomputed each read; a release flips `active‚Üíqueued` in the same txn and is idempotent (the batch tops up to the budget, so a re-read releases nothing new), and a queued row that became `keep`/mutual/ally/follows-back after release is **revoked** back to active. `keep` is a column enforced in the pure fns, never in the whitelist set. Suite 1211‚Üí**1224** (+13). **Out-of-band (2026-07-23 cost audit):** the daily-metrics discovery pull now IS the snapshot read (`ownedPrivate` on the pull + new idempotent `ingestPulledTweet`), killing a per-tweet double-read that was ~$0.09/day; replies dropped from the winner re-read; `discover()` try/caught. See the `workers/` table row + PHASE-HISTORY "discovery pull IS the snapshot". Two findings deferred to `plans/2026-07-23-cost-audit-followups.md` (CA.1 mention-inbox 50-cap data loss, CA.2 ledger under-count). **GR.2 ‚Äî harvester following mode** [xhigh, deps GR.1‚úì + HV.2‚úì, **$0**, extension-only] gives the ledger its client half: `HarvestMode` gains `'following'`, the scroll engine is reused unchanged, and `runHarvest`'s ingest param became a `ship(profile, store, outcome)` step whose `outcome.complete` (the stable-height break, and only that) decides whether the last `/x/following/rows` batch closes the run `done: true`. The pure cell reader is `extension/src/shared/userCell.ts` (fixture-tested, ¬ß7.27); `loggedInHandle()` refuses a run over someone else's list on a positive mismatch. Prior state, still current: **GR.1 ‚Äî following ledger: schema + ingest/ratchet routes** [xhigh, no deps, **$0**] **opened the GR lane**, the last one in Wave 3. New tables `following_runs` + `following` (migration **`0019`** ‚Äî the journal's first move since 0018) and a new `src/x/routes/following.ts` mounted right after `harvest`. One $0 DOM scrape of my own `/following` page yields BOTH sides (X renders a "Follows you" badge per row), so there is no API sync and no `follows.write` scope ‚Äî unfollowing stays manual in the X app and this layer only ever nudges. The load-bearing rule: **presence is ground truth, absence is only evidence when the scroll finished** ‚Äî batches update what they see, and only a run closed `done:true` **with `rowsSeen > 0`** reconciles (unseen `active|queued`‚Üí`gone`, unseen `done`‚Üí`confirmed`, seen `done`‚Üí`queued`). A zero-row close is stamped `completed_at` but never `complete`, so a broken selector cannot wipe the ledger. `first_seen_at` is the fill-only follow-date proxy (¬ß7.11); a `confirmed`/`gone` handle seen again revives to `active` without resetting it.
> This file exists so `/plan-feature` never re-scans the repo. It is the single
> pre-computed answer to "where does X live and how is it wired".
> **Maintenance rule:** any commit that adds/moves/deletes a file, route, table,
> worker, extension surface, or pattern MUST update the touched section here (and
> re-stamp the header). Every plan produced by `/plan-feature` ends with a
> docs-sync task that includes this file.

## 1. Thirty-second orientation

Single-user service (one human, one bearer token) with four goals and a **hard
scope ceiling** (a feature not serving one of these does not get built):

1. Schedule X posts a week ahead (calendar + 60s publisher worker).
2. Track metrics over time on every published post (daily 03:00 UTC once-only snapshot pass).
3. Voice library ‚Äî stash other people's tweets via $0 DOM scrape for style analysis.
4. Circles ‚Äî the people layer: CRM stages, conversations/open loops, relationship-aware drafting, Playbook, warmth (quests/digest/icebreakers).

Runtime: **Bun ‚â•1.1 + Hono** server on Hetzner (`https://stratus-narcis.duckdns.org`, systemd `stratus.service`, deployed via `scripts/deploy.sh`) + **Chrome MV3 side-panel extension** (Vite + React, loaded unpacked). State: **local SQLite via `bun:sqlite`** + Drizzle (`sqlite-core`), auto-migrated at boot. AI: xAI Grok via `src/grok/` (text `askGrok`, images `generateImages`). No queue, no Redis ‚Äî in-process `setInterval` workers.

Update the matching file when a tab changes. |

| `plans/` | 12 feature plans + `MASTERPLAN.md` (unified execution order, reasoning levels, waves, adaptations D1‚ÄìD10). Execution state: `.claude/skills/masterplan/STATE.md`. |

## 3. Server ‚Äî `src/`

### 3.1 Entry + shared (platform-agnostic) layer

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `src/app.ts` | Hono app. Order: CORS ‚Üí public `/healthz` ‚Üí `bearerAuth()` on `/x/*`, `/cost/*`, `/grok/*`, `/llm/*`, `/mcp` ‚Üí `cost` routes ‚Üí `mountX(app)` ‚Üí `mountGrok(app)` ‚Üí `mountLlm(app)` (always mounts ‚Äî unlike mountGrok) ‚Üí `mountMcp(app)` (after mountX so curated tools find routes). `import.meta.main` gates `Bun.serve` + `startXWorkers()` + SIGTERM/SIGINT drain (30s force-exit). Importing from tests never binds a port. |
| `src/middleware/auth.ts` | Bearer guard (`API_TOKEN`). |
| `src/middleware/cors.ts` | `chrome-extension://*` always allowed + `ALLOWED_ORIGINS`. |
| `src/middleware/costTracker.ts` | `makeOnCost(platform, {dailyBudgetUsd})` ‚Üí writes `cost_events`, platform-tagged; soft budget watchdog logs `BUDGET WATCHDOG`. Platform-agnostic ‚Äî never hardcode X here. **UI.5:** `dailyBudgetUsd` may be a **getter** (`number \| (() => number)`) resolved per read by `getDailyBudgetUsd` (used by the watchdog AND `/cost/*`), so a settings PATCH binds immediately; a throwing getter degrades to "no budget", never a 500. |
| `src/db/client.ts` | The one `bun:sqlite` Database (WAL, `foreign_keys=ON`, boot auto-migrate). **Synchronous driver** ‚Äî see ¬ß7 constraints. |
| `src/db/shared-schema.ts` | `cost_events` (platform free-text: `'x' \| 'grok' \| 'xai' \| 'openrouter'`; AI.1 added the union comment) + `app_settings` (UI.1 ‚Äî `key`/JSON `value`/`updatedAt` override rows; a missing row = the registry default). |
| `src/settings/store.ts` | UI.1 **platform-agnostic** settings store: sync read-through over `app_settings` (module-level `Map` cache + invalidate-on-write), `getSetting`/`resolveSetting`/`getAllValues(scope?)`/`setSettings`(validate-all ‚Üí one-txn upsert)/`resetSettings`. Takes a `SettingsRegistry` (never imports `src/x/*`, like `costTracker` takes `platform`). |
| `src/db/migrations/` | `0000`‚Äì`0014` + meta (`0013` = `app_settings`, UI.1; `0014` = RU.2 reply `source` + radar `variants`/`model`/`reply_draft_id`). `0000` carries the `content_pillars` seed `INSERT OR IGNORE` ‚Äî drizzle-kit generate drops seed INSERTs; re-check after every generate. biome-ignored (UI.1). |
| `src/routes/cost.ts` | `GET /cost/today` (per-platform spend + budget flags), `GET /cost/daily?days=` (zero-filled UTC series). |
| `src/routes/healthz.ts` | Public. 503 with `staleWorkers` when a heartbeat goes stale; reports `gitSha` from `.git-sha`; DB errors masked as `db_unreachable`. |
| `src/heartbeats.ts` | Worker heartbeat registry (`beat()` per tick; publisher stale >5min, dailyMetrics >25h). |
| `src/shared/replyBand.ts` | Canonical band classifier (hot/warm/skip/null) + `textLooksLikeReplyBait` ‚Äî shared server/extension (extension re-export shim). |
| `src/shared/channelSuggest.ts` | Keyword‚Üíchannel suggestion (word-boundary matching), shared server/extension. |
| `src/shared/activeTimes.ts` | A3.1 ‚Äî Active-times audience-heatmap pure core: `ActiveTimesGrid` ([col][row], col 0 = Mon), `parseHeatColors` (CSS ‚Üí min-max 0..1; grid-level alpha mode; >20% unparseable ‚Üí null), `audienceScoreFor` (getDay‚ÜîMon..Sun mapping + hour-row averaging), `gridsEqual` (Œµ 0.02), bounds `ACTIVE_TIMES_COLS/MIN_ROWS/MAX_ROWS` (A3.2 imports these). DOM extractor + re-export live extension-side (¬ß7.27). |
| `src/mcp.ts` | S2 platform-agnostic MCP bridge: per-request stateless `McpServer` + `WebStandardStreamableHTTPServerTransport` at `POST /mcp`; calls `registerXTools`. |
| `src/test.test.ts` | Grab-bag pure-function suite (best-times, annotateGaps, pinnedSince/buildPinnedWatch, md_to_schedule ladders‚Ä¶). New tests should go in per-area files instead. |
| `src/app.test.ts` | Pre-DB route guards: bearer 401s, CORS preflight, calendar/thread/drafter validation. |

### 3.2 LLM providers ‚Äî `src/grok/` (text+images) + `src/openrouter/` (AI.1) + `src/llm/` dispatcher (AI.2)

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `grok/client.ts` | `askGrok` ‚Äî ALL xAI text calls. `/v1/responses`, structured outputs via `text.format` json_schema (NOT `response_format`), `prompt_cache_key`, retry/auth, token pricing ‚Üí `cost_events` platform `'grok'`; warns on unknown model. |
| `grok/images.ts` | `generateImages` ‚Äî ALL xAI image calls. `grok-imagine-image` default ($0.02/img; `-quality` $0.05 opt-in), `response_format:b64_json` (never let a raw xAI URL reach the extension ‚Äî canvas taint), prefers response `usage.cost_in_usd_ticks` over the price table; platform `'xai'`. |
| `grok/pricing.ts` | Token + per-image price maps (`priceForImage`). |
| `grok/routes/ask.ts` | `POST /grok/ask` passthrough. |
| `grok/index.ts` | `mountGrok` (refuses to mount without `XAI_API_KEY`). |
| `openrouter/client.ts` | **AI.1** ‚Äî `askOpenRouter`, the ONE place all OpenRouter calls go (a second LLM provider, sibling to grok). `POST /api/v1/chat/completions` (OpenAI shape), structured outputs via `response_format.json_schema` (NOT xAI's `text.format`), `usage:{include:true}` + `provider:{require_parameters:true}` ALWAYS; **cost comes straight off `usage.cost` (USD) ‚Äî NO price table** (warns on a 2xx with tokens but no cost, ¬ß9.1); retry/auth/logCost mirror askGrok; `cost_events` platform `'openrouter'`; soft `OPENROUTER_DAILY_BUDGET_USD` watchdog (default $1.00, log-only). `DEFAULT_MODEL='anthropic/claude-sonnet-4.5'` (AI.2 settings own the real default); optional `fetchImpl` test seam; NO `promptCacheKey` (no OpenAI-compat field). INERT until AI.2 wires `askLLM`/`/llm` routes. |
| `openrouter/index.ts` | Re-exports only (`askOpenRouter`, `OpenRouterApiError`, `DEFAULT_MODEL`, types). No route/mount here ‚Äî `/llm/*` lives in `src/llm/` (AI.2). |
| `llm/ask.ts` | **AI.2** ‚Äî `askLLM(opts, {defaults})`, the provider dispatcher (¬ß7.1 extended: the ONE place picking grok vs openrouter; each provider keeps its own single entry point). Resolution `opts.provider ?? settings.provider`; merge precedence **opts > DB AI settings > call-site defaults** encoded once here (temperature/maxOutputTokens/reasoningEffort; model: openrouter‚Üí`opts.model ?? settings.openrouterModel`, grok‚Üí`opts.model` else askGrok's `grok-4.3`). A resolved provider whose env key is missing throws `LlmNotConfiguredError` ‚Äî **never a silent fallback**. Forwards `fetchImpl` only on the openrouter path, `promptCacheKey` only on grok. Also `llmConfigured()` (either key set ‚Äî the AI-layer runtime gate) / `llmProviderReady(p)` / pure `resolveProvider` / **`llmErrorPayload(err)`** (AI.5 ‚Äî shared HTTP mapping: `LlmNotConfiguredError`‚Üí503 `llm_not_configured`, `GrokApiError`/`OpenRouterApiError`‚Üí429/502 `grok_upstream_error`/`openrouter_upstream_error`, else null so routes keep their generic branch). **LIVE (AI.5 + AI.6)** ‚Äî call sites: replies single+batch, drafter, pillars/draft, voiceExtract, playbook extract-winners, digest, icebreaker. |
| `llm/settings.ts` | **AI.2** ‚Äî `getAiSettings`/`saveAiSettings`/`parseAiPatch` over `app_settings` key `'ai'` (REUSES UI.1's table, D1; NOT a registry key so the UI.1 store never touches it). Read-through, NO cache (loadDoctrine discipline). `AiSettings{provider,openrouterModel,temperature|null,maxOutputTokens|null,reasoningEffort|null}`, defaults `grok`/`anthropic/claude-sonnet-4.5`/nulls. Field-by-field `sanitize` (garbage/schema-drift row ‚Üí defaults). **NO API keys here** ‚Äî explorer/MCP-visible table (¬ß7.16, Decision 5); keys stay in env. |
| `llm/routes.ts` | **AI.2** ‚Äî `GET/PATCH /llm/settings` (+ `providers:{grok,openrouter}` env flags; PATCH 400 per field, 409 `provider_not_configured` picking openrouter without its key, returns full settings), `GET /llm/models` (OpenRouter's free list, in-memory 1h cache, 503 `openrouter_not_configured` keyless). |
| `llm/index.ts` | `mountLlm(app)` (**always mounts**, unlike mountGrok) + re-exports `askLLM`/`llmConfigured`/`llmProviderReady`/`LlmNotConfiguredError` + settings helpers/types. |

### 3.3 X slice ‚Äî `src/x/` (public surface = `index.ts` ONLY; nothing outside imports deeper)

**Primitives**

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `index.ts` | `mountX(app)` + `startXWorkers()` + re-export `registerXTools`. **Read this first for any wiring change ‚Äî mount order is load-bearing** (see ¬ß7 traps). LLM-gated mounts (**AI.6**): `replies`, `drafter`, `voiceExtract` only when `llmConfigured()` (EITHER `XAI_API_KEY` or `OPENROUTER_API_KEY`); `digest`/`playbook`/`pillars` mount always and check `llmConfigured()` at runtime (503); `images` stays `XAI_API_KEY`-only (Decision 6). **UI.4:** `startXWorkers` reads the two `appliesOn:'restart'` cadence knobs ONCE (`x.workers.publisherIntervalSec` ‚Üí `startPublisher({intervalMs})`, `x.workers.dailyMetricsHourUtc` ‚Üí `startDailyMetrics({hourUtc})`) and logs them ‚Äî no hot-reloading timers (decision 10). |
| `client.ts` | `xFetch` ‚Äî the ONE place all X API calls go (retries, RFC7807 parsing, rate-limit headers, `onCost`, `costHint`). Invariant #4. **CA.2 step 1:** logs `[cost-audit] ‚Ä¶ data=N includes.tweets=N includes.users=N` on 2xx reads carrying `includes` (expanded parents/authors `itemCount` never counted ‚Äî suspected ledger under-count); instrument-only, no `cost_usd` change until a 03:00 pass confirms. |
| `auth.ts` / `server.ts` / `token-store.ts` | OAuth2 PKCE; `bun run auth` callback server; single-row token store ‚Äî refresh-token rotation persisted BEFORE return, serialized by in-process promise-chain mutex (invariant #3 ‚Äî never reorder). |
| `endpoints.ts` | Typed wrappers: `getMe`, `getTweet`, `getTweetsByIds`, `searchRecent`, `getUserTweets`, `getUserMentions`, `createPost` (URL-surcharge + self-reply + self-quote gates), `deletePost`. Add one endpoint at a time, clamp `max_results` (invariant #5). `getUserMentions` takes `maxTotal` (CA.1) ‚Äî a TOTAL ceiling across pages; page size stays clamped by `maxResults`. |
| `fields.ts` / `errors.ts` / `pagination.ts` | Field defaults (`attachments` already included ‚Äî rides free), `XApiError`+classify, `paginate` async iterator (`perPageSleepMs` for search/all). |
| `pricing.ts` | X price table keyed off endpoint substrings; call sites pass `costHint` when the path can't tell. |
| `db/schema.ts` | All 34 X tables (¬ß4). Type-imports `NicheDoctrine` from `niche/defaults.ts` (type-only, no runtime cycle). |
| `settings/registry.ts` | UI.1 typed settings catalog: `SettingDef`, `SETTINGS_REGISTRY`, `validateSettingValue` (number/bool/string/enum/numberArray + sorted-unique), `settingsByGroup`. Implements the store's `SettingsRegistry` adapter + exports the **bound** `getSetting`/`resolveSetting`/`getAllValues`/`setSettings`/`resetSettings` ‚Äî consumers import these, never the store. **UI.2** groups: `doctrine` (**anchors3/anchors4/ladderSwitchAt only** ‚Äî reply band/week-%/2‚Äì10√ó are NICHE-owned; D2/D30c dropped the 3 dup keys UI.1 seeded), `quests` (originalsTarget/neglectedTargetsCount/neglectedTargetDays/launchAttendWindowMin), `display` (sparklineDays/leaderCount). **UI.3** groups (all `server`): `people` (mutualExchangeDays/allyExchangeDays/allyWindowDays ‚Äî stage thresholds; **NO targetBandMinX/MaxX ‚Äî those stay niche-owned**, the same D2 drop), `followups` (chainLiveMaxAgeH/dmReadyWindowDays/neglectedTargetDays/neglectedAllyDays/momentumWeeklyPct/reupMinAgeDays/reupMaxAgeDays/fanUnacknowledgedDays), `pinned` (staleDays/outperformRatio [fractional, step 0.5]), `digest` (neglectedCap). **UI.4** groups: `gates` (`minCellN` 5‚Äì100 default 20 = the Playbook cell gate; `bestTimeMinN` 1‚Äì20 default 3, **`mirrored`** ‚Äî the only mirrored UI.4 knob), `radar` (`draftTtlH` 6‚Äì168), `workers` (`dailyMetricsHourUtc`/`publisherIntervalSec`, both **`appliesOn:'restart'`**; `winnerRereadMinViews` [default from `envNumberDefault('WINNER_REREAD_MIN_VIEWS',500,‚Ä¶)` ‚Äî override row > env > baked, an out-of-range env value is warned and ignored] / `winnerRereadCap` 0‚Äì10, both read per daily run). Group render order = doctrine‚Üíquests‚Üípeople‚Üífollowups‚Üípinned‚Üídigest‚Üígates‚Üíradar‚Üíworkers‚Üídisplay. Store consumers: `routes/brief.ts`, `routes/followups.ts`, `routes/digest.ts`, `routes/playbook.ts`, `routes/metrics.ts`, `routes/radar.ts`, `workers/dailyMetrics.ts`, `index.ts::startXWorkers`, and (only impure DB module that reads the store) `people/store.ts::recomputePerson`. |
| `playground.ts` | `bun run play` scratch calls. |

**Domain modules (pure logic, bun-tested)**

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `conversations.ts` | C2 thread grouping/ranking (`buildThreads`/`rankThreads`/`isActionable`) ‚Äî no conversation table, regrouped per read. |
| `mentions.ts` | `pullMentions` ‚Äî since_id checkpoint = max stored tweet_id; incremental pulls page to `MENTIONS_HARD_CAP` 800 (CA.1 ‚Äî caller `maxResults` stays a total cap, cold pull stays the bounded 50); answered backfill; C1 person hooks. **UI.5:** page size comes from the separate `opts.pullMax` (`x.mentions.pullMax`); it must NOT be passed as `maxResults` ‚Äî that flag is what switches `maxTotal` off the 800 cap. |
| `playbook.ts` | C4/S0.x aggregations, all gated `DEFAULT_MIN_CELL_N` (n‚â•20): angles, pillar√óregister, structures, batch-vs-single (**RU.9:** `classifyReplyOrigin` takes a `postedTweetId‚Üíreply_drafts.source` map ‚Äî a draft-linked reply is `radar` iff `source='radar'`, else `single`; the radar text-match heuristic is now only the fallback for replies with NO draft link, i.e. pre-tooling history; **RL.7:** a 4th param `cannedTexts: ReadonlySet<string>` of normalized `reply_list_uses.renderedText` is checked LAST ‚Äî a canned use leaves no `reply_drafts` row, so rendered text is its only evidence; `ReplyOrigin` = `'single'|'radar'|'canned'`, `BatchVsSingle` gains a `canned` cell, and a reply that is both a posted draft and a text match counts once, as the draft), band calibration, relationship lift, media (S0.2), latency (S0.5), roster coverage (S0.7), idea payoff (S0.8), **personal-context lift (`buildMeEffectiveness`, ME.5 ‚Äî replies split by `contextSnapshot.me` present/absent; `withMe`/`withoutMe`/`totalMeasured`, clone of relationship lift + a `totalMeasured` field for the partition invariant)**, **model effectiveness (`buildModelEffectiveness`, AI.12 ‚Äî posted replies bucketed by raw `reply_drafts.model` string [`/` = provider, never parsed]; `{cells: ModelCell[], totalMeasured}`, cells most-sampled-first, each independently gated; **no lift line** ‚Äî buckets only, no baseline pair; the OpenRouter-experiment judge)**, **timeline opportunity funnel (`buildTimelineFunnel`, HV.5 ‚Äî ¬ß12, NOT ¬ß11 which AI.12 took; `TimelineSeenRow{tweetId,views,comments,text,tweetTimeMs|null,capturedAtMs}` + `deriveTimelineBand` [ageMin = capturedAt‚àítweetTime, vpm = views/max(ageMin,1), bait = `textLooksLikeReplyBait`, fed to shared `classifyBand`] ‚Üí `{cells: FunnelCell[], totalSeen, totalReplied}`; `TimelineBand = Band | 'unknown'` where **`'unknown'` = no tweet time (no age ‚áí no velocity ‚áí nothing to classify) and NEVER folds into the real `null` band**; rows are deduped to their **first sighting** (earliest `capturedAtMs`) inside the pure fn too, so a re-scrolled viral thread can't re-band itself; per-cell gate on `seen`, `rate = replied/seen` null under it)**. |
| `quests.ts` | C9 daily quests (vacuous-done contract ‚Äî a quiet day never breaks the streak). **GR.8:** `QuestInputs.originalsTarget?` (default 1) is the one commitment hook ‚Äî additive, so an input without it behaves exactly as before, and the `original` label pluralizes only above 1. A commitment's floor is 1, so it can only ever RAISE a bar (no streak already on the books can be retroactively broken). |
| `digest.ts` | C9 Sunday digest facts assembly (pure; one LLM narration in the route, cached in `digests`). **ME.5:** `DigestGoal` + `DigestFacts.goals` (active `me_goals` + progress; null when none, passthrough in `buildDigestFacts`). **AI.6:** `DIGEST_INSTRUCTIONS` ‚Üí exported `DIGEST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `digest`, `{{FACTS}}` at the tail); `buildDigestInput(facts, template = DIGEST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE)` substitutes via local split/join (no registry import ‚Äî cycle) ‚Äî byte-identical to the old concatenation. **GR.9:** `DigestFacts.scorecard: DigestScorecard | null` (= goals.ts `Scorecard` + `prevScore`/`delta`). Unlike every other fact it is NOT a passthrough ‚Äî `buildDigestFacts` calls `computeScorecard` itself, feeding it the `quests`/`activity` numbers it just derived (the `conversionRate` precedent), so a grade can never disagree with the facts it grades; the route supplies only what rows can't say via `scorecardInputs` (`daysWithOriginal`, `daysInWeek`, `repliesTargetWeek`, `targetReplyPct`, `goalVerdicts`, `prevScore`). **The WHOLE card is null under the gate** (`sufficient===false` or a null score), not just the score ‚Äî the narration's skip-nulls rule then covers it, and component scores over a 2-day week never reach Grok. `DIGEST_INSTRUCTIONS`/the template are untouched (¬ß7.15 ‚Äî the facts block is already the variable tail). |
| `conversion.ts` | S0.1 profile-visit ‚Üí follow conversion math. |
| `people/stage.ts` | Stage engine: stranger‚Üínoticed‚Üíengaged‚Üíresponded‚Üímutual (‚â•2 exchange days)‚Üíally (‚â•4/60d); ratchets up only. **UI.3:** the thresholds are `StageThresholds`/`STAGE_DEFAULTS` ‚Äî `computeStage(events, now, thresholds=STAGE_DEFAULTS)`; `store.ts::recomputePerson` reads the `people`-group overrides (only affects future recomputes ‚Äî the ratchet never demotes). **NT.2:** `PERSON_EVENT_TYPES` gained `their_like`/`their_repost`/`their_follow` and they are in **no** stage set (not NOTICED/INBOUND/OUTBOUND) ‚Äî engagement is not reciprocity, so 50 likes + a follow is still `stranger` (C10 decision 1, matrix-tested; do not re-litigate). |
| `people/store.ts` | All people writes: `upsertPerson` (fill-only default, overwrite for profile scrapes), `logPersonEvents`/`safeLogPersonEvents` (deterministic ids `type:ref_table:ref_id` + INSERT OR IGNORE), `loadRelationshipFacts(Safe)`. |
| `people/relationship.ts` | C3 relationship block render (server-stamped, variable-tail). |
| `people/angles.ts` | Per-person angle crosstab. |
| `people/followups.ts` | C5 classifier: chain_live > dm_ready > neglected_target > neglected_ally > momentum; S0.6 `pickReupCandidate`; snooze keys `kind:handle` / `reup:<tweetId>`. **UI.3:** the windows are settings-backed via defaulted params ‚Äî `classifyFollowups(inputs, windows=FOLLOWUP_DEFAULTS)` (chain/dm/target/ally), `momentumInflection(pts, now, {weeklyPctThreshold?})`, `fanUnacknowledged(fan, now, unackDays?)`; the route reads the `followups` group and the reup-age SQL bounds. |
| `connections.ts` | **GR.3** ‚Äî following-curation logic (pure, followups.ts style: no DB, no clock, no `Math.random`). Constants `GRACE_DAYS=7`/`UNFOLLOW_WINDOW_MS=6h`/`WINDOW_CAP_MIN=15`/`WINDOW_CAP_MAX=18`/`DAILY_CEILING=40`/`MARK_LOOKBACK_MS=24h`. `CurationRow` (structural ‚Äî a `following` row satisfies it), `rankForUnfollow` (oldest `firstSeenAt` first, `listPosition` desc tie-break, handle asc to make it total; non-mutating), `eligibleForUnfollow(rows, whitelist, now)` (`active`+`!followsBack`+`!keep`+`‚àâwhitelist`+past-grace, ranked), `reviewQueued(rows, whitelist)` ‚Üí `{held, revoked}` (a `queued` row that became `keep`/mutual/ally/follows-back after release is **revoked** back to active), `releaseBudget(marks, now, rand)` ‚Üí `{budget, windowCap, windowUsed, dailyUsed, dailyCeiling}` (jittered cap once per call, window count subtracted, `dailyUsed‚â•DAILY_CEILING`‚Üí0; **marks = completed unfollows only, never releases** ‚Äî a queued-never-done row eats no budget). Consumed only by `GET /following/queue`. |
| `monitor.ts` | **GR.5** ‚Äî activity monitor (pure, connections.ts style: no DB, no clock, no `Math.random`). `MonitorRule` (5-union) / `MonitorSeverity` (`info\|warn\|critical`) / `MonitorAlert {rule, severity, message, evidence}`; every threshold an exported constant (`POST_BURST_MAX=4`/`POST_PAIR_WINDOW_MS=20m`, `REPLY_BURST_WARN=10`/`_CRITICAL=15`/`_WINDOW_MS=1h`/`_LOOKBACK_MS=3h`, `NEAR_DUPLICATE_THRESHOLD=0.8`/`_WINDOW_MS=14d`/`SHINGLE_SIZE=3`, `UNFOLLOW_CHURN_WARN=25`, `SCHEDULE_CLUSTER_MS=45m`, `MAX_LISTED_PAIRS=5` ‚Äî all opening guesses). `UNFOLLOW_CHURN_WINDOW_MS` **is** `connections.ts`'s `MARK_LOOKBACK_MS` and the critical threshold **is** its `DAILY_CEILING` ‚Äî imported, never redeclared, so the queue's cap and the alert can't disagree. `normalizeForShingles` (lowercase ‚Üí strip URLs ‚Üí strip @handles ‚Üí strip punctuation+emoji ‚Üí split; order matters or the URL shatters into words) + `shingleJaccard` (a post shorter than `SHINGLE_SIZE` is its own single shingle, else two identical one-word posts read 0%). Rules `postBurst`/`replyBurst`/`nearDuplicate`/`unfollowChurn`/`scheduleCluster` each return `MonitorAlert \| null` ‚Äî **one alert per rule**, so the set is keyable; `runMonitor(inputs)` composes them severity-desc (stable sort ‚áí rule order within a severity) and `worstOf(alerts)` is the envelope's `worst`. `replyBurst` finds the DENSEST hour in the lookback (two-pointer `peakInWindow`), not the last hour ‚Äî a burst that ended 90 min ago is still what X saw. |
| `goals.ts` | **GR.7** ‚Äî accountability core (pure, monitor.ts style: no DB, no clock). `goalPacing(goal, current, actualPerDay, now)` ‚Üí `{current, pctComplete, daysLeft, requiredPerDay, actualPerDay, verdict, projectedAt}`; verdict is a **6-union** ‚Äî `unknown` covers BOTH "no current value" (¬ß7.11) and "no deadline" (no pace to hold), so nothing is ever graded 'behind' on missing data. Ratios `AHEAD_RATIO=1.1`/`ON_PACE_RATIO=0.8`. `nextGoalStatus` = the lazy ratchet (¬ß7.10): active‚Üí`achieved` on target, active‚Üí`missed` once the deadline passes **even with an unknown current** (a date is a fact about the calendar; one PATCH undoes it), terminal statuses never move. `COMMITMENT_KEYS` = `replies|originals` + **`COMMITMENT_QUEST_KEY`** ‚Äî the diary records originals under the SINGULAR quest key `original` (quests.ts), and this map is the only place that mismatch is resolved. `commitmentDebt(streakRows, key, activeSinceDayKey, todayKey)` ‚Üí `{missedLast7, missedLast30, trackedLast7, tier 0‚Äì3}`: window ends YESTERDAY (today is still in progress), days before `activeSince` count as nothing, a missing diary row IS a miss. `computeScorecard` (GR.9's consumer) ‚Äî five 0‚Äì100 components weighted 30/20/25/15/10, null components drop out and the rest reweight, `sufficient=false` (score null) under `SCORECARD_MIN_DAYS=4`; `VERDICT_SCORE` maps `unknown ‚Üí null` so an unmeasurable goal is excluded, not failed. Every constant is exported and mirrored nowhere. |
| `people/sightings.ts` | C6 hover-capture ingest (once/day/handle event + snapshot gates). |
| `people/engagements.ts` | **NT.2** ‚Äî C10 notification-harvest ingest (sightings.ts mirror). `MAX_ENGAGEMENTS_PER_BATCH=50`, `EngagementKind` = like\|repost\|follow (the parser's `'other'` is dropped client-side and is deliberately not representable), `dedupeEngagements` (key `kind:handle:targetText`, freshest wins), `engagementEventId` (`their_like:notif:<handle>:<tweetId>` ‚Üí day-bucket `‚Ä¶:<YYYY-MM-DD>` when unresolved ‚Üí `their_follow:notif:<handle>` once ever), pure `matchTargetTweetId(snippet, posts)` (collapsed-whitespace **prefix** match, ‚â•20 chars or null) + DB wrapper `resolveTargetTweetId`, `recordEngagements` ‚Üí `{received, processed, skipped, events}` (fill-only upsert `source:'notification'`, INSERT OR IGNORE events with `refTable/refId: null`, own-post window loaded **once per batch** and not at all for a follow-only batch, `recomputePerson` once per distinct handle = watermarks only). **NT.3:** `ENGAGEMENT_KINDS` + the `isEngagementKind` guard live here beside the union (`isStage`/`isFollowupKind` idiom) ‚Äî `POST /x/people/engagements` is their only caller and the enforcement point for the parser's `'other'`. |
| `people/icebreakers.ts` | C9 grounding renderer (refusal ladder BEFORE key check: 404 ‚Üí 422 no_shared_context). **AI.6:** `ICEBREAKER_INSTRUCTIONS` ‚Üí exported `ICEBREAKER_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `icebreaker`, `{{GROUNDING}}` at the tail); `buildIcebreakerInput(grounding, template = ICEBREAKER_PROMPT_TEMPLATE)` substitutes via local split/join ‚Äî byte-identical to the old concatenation. `IcebreakerGroundingInputs` is the shape `loadIcebreakerGrounding` (in `routes/people.ts`) assembles; **A3.9's DM drafter reuses that exact loader** (decision 8). |
| `people/dm.ts` | **A3.9** PURE DM-draft core: `DM_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `dm`), `buildDmPrompt(grounding, idea, purpose, template=DM_PROMPT_TEMPLATE)` (inline split/join over `{{GROUNDING}}`/`{{IDEA}}`/`{{PURPOSE}}`, absent idea/purpose ‚Üí labeled sentinel; language clause in the stable prefix ‚Äî decision 13), `DM_SCHEMA {dm}`, `parseDm`. **Never imports `renderPrompt`/a route** ‚Äî the registry imports this module for the `dm` default, so a back-import cycles (the RL.4 rule). |
| `articles/prompt.ts` | **A3.12** PURE article-assist core (registry default, key `article` ‚Üí 13 keys): `ARTICLE_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (byte-synced with `article prompt.md` ‚Äî persona HARDCODED, so the prefix is byte-static; language clause in the prefix), `ARTICLE_ASSIST_MODES`/`isArticleAssistMode`, `ASSIST_SCHEMAS` per mode (outline `{title,subtitle,sections:[{heading,beats[]}]}` ¬∑ section/polish `{markdown}` ¬∑ full `{title,subtitle,markdown}`), `parseAssist(mode,raw)` (truncation-safe null, the parsePostDrafts discipline), `buildArticleAssistInput(mode, ctx, template=ARTICLE_PROMPT_TEMPLATE)` (renders PILLARS/WINNERS/GUIDANCE/ARTICLE/INSTRUCTION at the tail; mode + idea/heading/selection compose INSTRUCTION so any-language input never shifts the cache prefix), `renderArticleState` (body clipped head+tail at `MAX_ARTICLE_BODY_IN_PROMPT`=6000). Imports ONLY `grok/index` (GrokMessage), `posts/pillars` (renderPillars/DEFAULT_PILLARS/PillarDef), `posts/prompt` (WinnerPost type) ‚Äî **never a route/registry** (the registry imports it for the default; a back-import cycles, RL.4 rule). |
| `niche/defaults.ts` | **N0.1** ‚Äî lowest niche layer (imports nothing from prompt/route/store, pillars.ts pattern). `NicheDoctrine` (5 knobs), `DEFAULT_DOCTRINE` (10/20/70/2/10), `Niche` type, `DEFAULT_NICHE` (`builder`; persona/beliefs/replyPersona lifted **verbatim** from post ¬ß1/¬ß5 + reply "Who I am", description from `src/my_niche.md` ‚Äî post ¬ß1/¬ß5 moved at N.3, reply "Who I am" moved at N.4; all guarded byte-exact by the equivalence fixtures in `src/test.test.ts`), `NICHE_SLUG_RE` (=PILLAR_SLUG_RE), `resolveDoctrine` (lenient field-by-field: finite positive wins, else default). |
| `niche/store.ts` | **N0.1** ‚Äî only reader of `niches`: `loadActiveNiche()` (active row else `DEFAULT_NICHE` when none), `loadActiveNicheSafe()` (never throws ‚Üí default, ¬ß7.8), `loadDoctrine()` (resolveDoctrine of the safe active niche). **Post-side consumers wired at N.3** (drafter + pillars/draft), **reply side at N.4** (replies single + batch); **doctrine wired at N.5** ‚Äî `loadDoctrine()` feeds `targetBand` multipliers + brief reply quota/ratio (voice, brief, followups, playbook, digest). |
| `me/profile.ts` | **ME.1** ‚Äî pure Me/profile layer (relationship.ts pattern: no DB, callers pass `now`). `ME_KINDS`/`GOAL_KINDS`, window consts (`EMOTION_WINDOW_DAYS=7`/`EVENT_WINDOW_DAYS=30`, inclusive boundary; facts/notes evergreen; `pinned` overrides window+cap), per-kind caps + render hard-caps (`MAX_POST_LINES=14`/`MAX_POST_CHARS=1200`, brief `‚â§3`/`300`), `ME_INSTRUCTION`/`ME_BRIEF_INSTRUCTION` (instruction rides INSIDE the block, ¬ß7.18), `selectEntriesForPrompt`, `goalProgress`/`resolveGoals` (followers ‚Üê account_snapshots value, mrr/custom ‚Üê manual currentValue; null when no data), `renderMeContext`/`renderMeBrief` (`''` when empty ‚Üí no injection ‚Üí prompts byte-identical). Loader `loadMeContextSafe` wired at **ME.2** (`routes/me.ts`); **ME.3** injects the rendered block at all three draft-prompt tails (post drafter + reply single + reply batch). |
| `niche/wizard.ts` | **N0.8** ‚Äî pure wizard module (pillarDraft.ts pattern): `NICHE_WIZARD_SCHEMA` (structured-outputs `{slug,label,description,persona,beliefs,replyPersona,pillars[3],channels[‚â§5 w/ keywords]}`), `buildNicheWizardInput(description)` (instruction+anatomy prefix, DEFAULT_NICHE+DEFAULT_PILLARS as the in-prompt EXAMPLE, user description at the variable TAIL ¬ß7.15), `parseNicheProposal(raw)` (lenient: coerces slugs to kebab-case, enforces exactly-3 distinct pillars + required non-empty text + length ceilings 120/10000 mirroring the CRUD routes; a malformed channel is dropped not fatal; junk/bad-slug/wrong-count ‚Üí null). Consumed only by `POST /x/niche/draft`. |
| `posts/prompt.ts` | `POST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (byte-synced with `post prompt.md`) + drafter helpers, `buildPostDraftsSchema(slugs)`. **N.3:** `PERSONA_PLACEHOLDER`/`BELIEFS_PLACEHOLDER`; `BuildPostDraftOptions.persona?/beliefs?` (default `DEFAULT_NICHE`) substituted FIRST, in place. **ME.3:** `BuildPostDraftOptions.meContext?` appended at the variable tail before `guidance` (empty ‚Üí no change). **AI.3:** `BuildPostDraftOptions.template?` ‚Äî the registry-loaded body (default `POST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE`, so callers/tests untouched). |
| `posts/pillars.ts` | `DEFAULT_PILLARS`, `parsePillar`. |
| `posts/manualReconcile.ts` | **A3.6** ‚Äî pure matcher `matchManualRows(manual, published) ‚Üí {scheduledPostId, tweetId}[]` linking hand-pasted tweets to their calendar rows (the impure wrapper is `reconcileManualPosts` in `workers/dailyMetrics.ts`). Candidates: published ORIGINALS (`isReply===false`) not yet linked (`scheduledPostId===null`); a link needs collapsed-whitespace text equality (`replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim()`) AND `postedAt ‚àà [scheduledFor ‚àí 1h, scheduledFor + 7d]` (edges inclusive). Global greedy over `\|postedAt ‚àí scheduledFor\|` (nearest first, stable-sort tie = manual-row order) so each tweet AND each row link at most once ‚Äî the harvest replies-reconcile discipline (`matchUnlinkedDraft`). Exports the window consts `RECONCILE_WINDOW_BEFORE_MS`/`AFTER_MS`. Empty-collapsed text never matches. No DB, no clock. |
| `posts/threadPrompt.ts` | **AI.7** ‚Äî thread drafter (pure): `THREAD_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (byte-synced with `thread prompt.md`; post ¬ß0‚Äì¬ß5 verbatim + thread job/output), `buildThreadDraftSchema(slugs)` (`{pillar enum, tweets string[]}` ‚Äî **no minItems/maxItems**, N.8/RU.3 rejection-risk convention; count steered by prompt), `parseThreadDraft(raw, slugs) ‚Üí {pillar, tweets, overLong}|null` (‚â•2 tweets, bad pillar ‚Üí null, 280-over `overLong` positions computed not rejected), `buildThreadDraftInput(opts)` (persona/beliefs in place; pillar+tweetCount+idea folded into the single `{{FEW_SHOT}}`/`{{IDEA}}` tail ‚Äî no `{{PILLAR}}` token; meContext+guidance appended). Imports only types/consts from `posts/prompt.ts` (no cycle). |
| `posts/rewritePrompt.ts` | **AI.8** ‚Äî rewrite assist (pure, **TS-only ‚Äî Decision 9, no `.md`/byte-sync**): `REWRITE_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (`{{DRAFT}}`/`{{INSTRUCTION}}` at the tail; **no persona/pillar token** ‚Üí cache bucket unaffected by niche), `REWRITE_SCHEMA` (static `{variants:[{text, kind}]}`, kind enum `tightened|rehooked|restructured`, **no minItems/maxItems**), `MAX_VARIANT_LENGTH=560`, `parseRewrite(raw, maxLen=560) ‚Üí RewriteVariant[]|null` (null on malformed `variants`; empty/over-long/unknown-kind entries dropped ‚Äî array may be `[]`), `buildRewriteInput({draft, instruction?, template?})` (split/join $-safe; missing instruction ‚Üí `(none ‚Äî just sharpen it)`). No DB, no niche import. |
| `posts/ideasPrompt.ts` | **AI.9** ‚Äî idea generator (pure, **TS-only ‚Äî Decision 9, no `.md`/byte-sync**): `IDEAS_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (`{{PILLARS}}`/`{{WINNERS}}`/`{{STEER}}` at the tail; **no persona/belief token** ‚Üí cache bucket niche-independent even though the rendered pillars are niche-scoped, since pillars sit at the variable tail), `IDEAS_SCHEMA` (static `{ideas:[{text,pillar,angle}]}`, angle enum `observation|stance|story|question`, **`pillar` a FREE string not enum-bound** so a mis-tag is nulled not dropped; **no minItems/maxItems**), `MAX_IDEA_TEXT=500`/`MAX_IDEA_COUNT=10`, `parseIdeaProposals(raw, allowedSlugs, maxCount=10) ‚Üí IdeaProposal[]|null` (null on malformed `ideas`; empty/over-long/unknown-angle entries dropped; a pillar outside `allowedSlugs` ‚Üí **null, not dropped**; clamped to maxCount ‚Äî array may be `[]`), `buildIdeasInput({pillars?, winners, steer?, count?, template?})` (split/join $-safe; count folds into the {{STEER}} block like threadPrompt folds tweetCount; empty winners/steer ‚Üí placeholder text). No DB, no niche import. |
| `posts/pillarDraft.ts` | AI pillar proposal (never persisted directly). **N.3:** hardcoded compact `PERSONA` deleted ‚Äî `BuildPillarDraftOptions.persona?` (default `DEFAULT_NICHE.persona`); the route passes niche.persona+description. **AI.5:** the persona+format block is now `PILLAR_DRAFT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `pillar-draft`) with `{{PERSONA}}` (optional, in-place first) + `{{EXISTING_PILLARS}}`/`{{JOB}}` (required); `BuildPillarDraftOptions.template?`; the job strings stay code-built. |
| `replies/prompt.ts` | `REPLY_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (byte-synced with `reply prompt.md`; **RU.1**: 3 variants, one per angle extends/contrarian/debate), `buildGrokInput`, `buildBatchGrokInput` (**AI.5**: renders the standalone `REPLY_BATCH_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` ‚Äî the heading-slicing `sharedVoiceBlock`/`batchReplyHead`/`VOICE_BLOCK_END` machinery is GONE; the batch default embeds the reply default's voice block verbatim, locked by the anti-drift test in `src/test.test.ts`; `{{POSTS}}`/`{{IDEA}}` substitute at the tail with the token-missing fallbacks preserved for pre-token overrides; the C3 relationship note rides inside the POSTS value; **RU.3**: 3 variants/post, `BatchReply={tweetId,variants[]}`, `parseBatchReplies` validates ‚â•1 variant/entry), `parseContext`/`parseBatchTweets` (NEVER accept `relationship`/`guidance`/`niche` from clients ‚Äî whitelist builders), `BATCH_REPLY_SCHEMA` (`{replies:[{id,variants:[{text,angle}]}]}`). **N.4:** "Who I am" body ‚Üí `{{REPLY_PERSONA}}` (`REPLY_PERSONA_PLACEHOLDER`); `buildGrokInput`/`buildBatchGrokInput` gain trailing `opts?: {replyPersona?}` (default `DEFAULT_NICHE.replyPersona`), substituted FIRST/token-tolerant via `substituteReplyPersona` (batch: over the effective template before POSTS/IDEA land); `PostContext.niche?: {slug}` server-stamped. **ME.3:** `PostContext.me?` server-stamped (parseContext allowlist never accepts it) ‚Äî `buildGrokInput` appends it at the tail after relationship (order relationship‚Üíme‚Üíguidance); `buildBatchGrokInput`'s opts bag gains `meBrief?`, appended ONCE per batch after guidance. **AI.3/AI.5:** BOTH builders' opts bags carry `template?` (registry body; per-request `override` still beats it). |
| `replyLists/engine.ts` | **RL.1** ‚Äî canned-reply engine (pure, followups.ts style: no DB, no clock, no `Math.random` ‚Äî callers inject `rng`). `MAX_REPLY_LENGTH=280`, `TEMPLATE_VARS` (`name`/`first_name`/`handle`), `DEFAULT_HUMANIZER` (prefix .25 / suffix .20 / lowercase .15 / drop-period .10 / typo .05 ‚Äî opening guesses; per-list JSON overrides), `parseHumanizerConfig` (lenient field-by-field, **null ONLY on a non-object** ‚Äî that's what lets RL.2's CRUD 400 an invalid humanizer) + `resolveHumanizer`, `renderTemplate` (a missing var takes ONE adjacent separator with it ‚Üí "Thank you!"; unknown `{foo}` verbatim; emoji/flags stripped from the name), `templateVars`/`availableVarsFor`, `pickItem` (anti-repeat: var-needing items deprioritized, `min(n-1, floor(n/2))` most-recent excluded, uniform pick among the rest ‚Äî no repeat at n‚â•2), `humanize` (**fixed `HUMANIZE_DRAWS`=10 draws whether or not a step fires**, so a stubbed sequence maps to steps by position; names/handles/`@`/`#`/links are protected spans never typo'd; an overflowing prefix/suffix is skipped, never truncated), `composeReply`. |
| `replyLists/generate.ts` | **RL.4** ‚Äî reply-list AI item generator (pure, **TS-only ‚Äî Decision 9, no `.md`/byte-sync**): `REPLY_LIST_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `reply-list`; `{{COUNT}}`/`{{REQUEST}}`/`{{EXISTING_ITEMS}}` all required and all at the tail ‚Äî **no persona token**, so the cacheable prefix is niche-independent and the route's cache key needs no `:slug:updatedAtMs` suffix, same as `ideas`/`rewrite`), `REPLY_LIST_GEN_SCHEMA` (`{items:[{text}]}`, no minItems/maxItems ‚Äî the strict-mode rejection-risk convention), `buildListGenInput({prompt, count?, existingItems?, template?})` (split/join $-safe; empty list ‚Üí `(none yet ‚Äî this list is empty)`; existing items capped at 30), `parseGeneratedItems(raw, maxCount=30) ‚Üí {text}[]|null` (**null only when `items` is missing/not an array**; empty + >`MAX_REPLY_LENGTH` entries dropped; **dedupe key is lowercased + whitespace-collapsed**, since casing-only twins defeat the anti-repeat pick; `[]` is a legal "nothing survived" the route 502s on). `DEFAULT_GENERATED_ITEMS`=12 / `MAX_GENERATED_ITEMS`=30 / `MAX_GEN_PROMPT_LEN`=2000. |
| `prompts/registry.ts` | **AI.3** ‚Äî the editable-prompt catalog: `PROMPT_KEYS` (**A3.12: 13 keys ‚Äî `reply`/`reply-batch`/`post`/`thread`/`rewrite`/`ideas`/`voice-extract`/`pillar-draft`/`digest`/`icebreaker`/`reply-list`/`dm`/`article`** ‚Äî new keys append at the end; defaults from pure modules, `ideas` from `posts/ideasPrompt.ts`, `reply-list` from `replyLists/generate.ts`, `dm` from `people/dm.ts`, `article` from `articles/prompt.ts`), `isPromptKey`, `PROMPT_SPECS` (name/description/`defaultBody` = the byte-synced templates + `required`/`optional` placeholder sets; **defaults import from PURE modules only ‚Äî a route-file import would cycle**), `loadPrompt(key)`/`loadPromptSafe` (¬ß7.8 ‚Äî `prompt_overrides` row else default; row presence IS `customized`; sha-8 `cacheKey`, call sites append the niche `:slug:updatedAtMs` suffix), `validatePromptBody` (`{ok,missing,unknown}` ‚Äî required must survive an edit, niche placeholders optional/token-tolerant, unknown `{{A_Z}}` deduped warning), `renderPrompt` (split/join, $-safe; for later-task call sites), `promptCacheKey`. Imports the prompt modules for defaults incl. `digest.ts`/`people/icebreakers.ts` (AI.6 ‚Äî both pure-ish, no registry import; no cycle: routes ‚Üí registry ‚Üí templates). |
| `voice/extractPrompt.ts` | **AI.5** ‚Äî pure ¬ß8.3 extraction pieces moved out of `routes/voiceExtract.ts` (registry-cycle avoidance): `EXTRACT_PROMPT_TEMPLATE` (registry default, key `voice-extract`, `{{TWEET_TEXT}}` at the tail ‚Äî renders byte-identical to the old `EXTRACT_PROMPT_PREFIX + text`), `TEMPLATE_SCHEMA`, `TEMPLATE_LENGTHS`/`TemplateLength`/`ExtractedTemplate`, `parseExtractedTemplate`, `TEMPLATE_EXTRACT_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS`. Consumed by `routes/voiceExtract.ts` + `routes/playbook.ts`. |
| `data/inspect.ts` | S1 read-only core: second `{readonly:true}` connection (`:memory:` falls back to primary), whitelist from Drizzle exports (**`tokens` excluded entirely**), `readTable` (validated identifiers, escaped LIKE), `runSelect` (single-statement SELECT/WITH, 500-row cap), `describeTable`. Reused by MCP schema tools. |
| `mcp.ts` | S2 `registerXTools` ‚Äî 23 tools: 3 schema (inspect core), 15 curated (in-process `app.request` with forwarded bearer; `x_digest` forces `factsOnly`; **N0.2 added `x_niche`** ‚Üí `GET /x/niche`; **M1.6 added `x_me`** ‚Üí `GET /x/me`; **GR.5 added `x_monitor`** ‚Üí `GET /x/monitor`, no inputs; **GR.7 added `x_goals`** ‚Üí `GET /x/goals?tzOffsetMin=`, read-only ‚Äî goal WRITES stay out by design, ME.6's rule that a bad target steers every draft; **UI.4 added `x_settings`** ‚Üí `GET /x/settings`, the whole knob catalog with values/ranges/isDefault), 5 write ($0 only; **UI.4 added `x_update_setting`** ‚Üí `PATCH /x/settings` `{[key]:value}`, same registry validation as the UI so a ceiling refuses with the 400 surfaced in the tool result; `x_draft_post` hard-codes `status:'draft'`; **M1.6 added `x_add_me_entry`** ‚Üí `POST /x/me/entries`, zod enum restricts `kind` to the 4 ME_KINDS ‚Äî no goal write, journal only). |

**Workers ‚Äî `src/x/workers/`**

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `publisher.ts` | Tick every `x.workers.publisherIntervalSec` (**UI.4**, default 60s, `appliesOn:'restart'` ‚Äî `startXWorkers` passes `intervalMs` once at boot). Claim txn (`pending‚Üípublishing` committed BEFORE `createPost`) ‚Üí finalize; 4xx‚Üí`failed`, 5xx/network ‚Üí stuck `publishing` (ambiguous, shouted every tick, reconcile resolves). Threads: self-replies ~500ms apart, one bad segment freezes the rest (`thread_frozen`); re-verifies self-quote ownership. |
| `dailyMetrics.ts` | Fires at `x.workers.dailyMetricsHourUtc` (**UI.4**, default 03:00 UTC, `appliesOn:'restart'`): getMe ‚Üí `account_snapshots` (1/UTC-day, + `pinned_tweet_id`); since_id discovery of own tweets ‚Äî the pull requests `ownedPrivate` so it **IS the snapshot** (`ingestPulledTweet`: row+snapshot+retire in one idempotent txn; the read is already billed, so idempotency not retire-before-read guards invariant #7). `snapshotDue` is now the **leftover backstop** (rows below the checkpoint / failed batches ‚Äî retires batch BEFORE writing snapshots, $0 in steady state); `fullScan` keeps the old cheap-pull-then-age-split-read (30-day private-field window); winner re-read (**UI.4**: floor/cap are `x.workers.winnerRereadMinViews`/`‚Ä¶Cap`, read at the START of each run ‚Äî NOT restart-scoped ‚Äî or overridden via `RunOptions`; `cap<=0` returns BEFORE the candidate query and its claim write; **originals only** `isReply=false`, claim pollCount 1‚Üí2 before the billed call); `discover()` try/caught so a pull failure degrades to two-phase, never skips snapshot+reread+mentions; `pullMentions`. **A3.6:** `reconcileManualPosts(result)` runs try/caught right after `discover` (before `snapshotDue`) ‚Äî links the pasted tweets discovery just ingested back to their `manual`/`posted`-but-unlinked calendar rows via the `matchManualRows` matcher (`posts/manualReconcile.ts`), both selects bounded to 30 d (typed `gte(col, Date)`, not raw sql), one sync txn per match stamping `scheduled_posts.posted_tweet_id` + `status='posted'` (manual‚Üíposted, posted stays posted) + `posts_published.scheduled_post_id`; $0 (SQL over already-billed rows), inserts NOTHING into posts_published so the since_id checkpoint is untouched (the trap), a failure never fails the run. New `RunResult.manualLinked`, logged `manualLinked=n`. See PHASE-HISTORY "discovery pull IS the snapshot" (2026-07-23). |

### 3.4 HTTP routes ‚Äî `src/x/routes/` (all under `/x`, bearer-guarded unless noted)

| Router file | Endpoints (method path ‚Äî one-line semantics) |
|---|---|
| `brief.ts` | `GET /brief` ‚Äî Today-tab payload: KPI+sparkline, yesterday, leaders, plan+annotated gaps (S0.4), reply quota, ratio, spend, quests+streak (C9), pinnedWatch (S0.9). `?tzOffsetMin=` local-day; spend stays UTC. Pure helpers `pinnedSince`/`buildPinnedWatch` live here. **N.5:** the old `REPLY_TARGET`/`WEEK_REPLY_TARGET_PCT` consts are gone ‚Äî reply quota/ratio target + the target-roster band all read `loadDoctrine()` (one sync SELECT/request). **GR.6:** a `monitor: {alerts, worst}` block, built by calling the monitor route's exported `loadMonitorInputs(now)` inside the big `Promise.all` + `runMonitor`/`worstOf` ‚Äî never a second copy of that SQL (the `loadBestTimeCells` precedent). **GR.8:** two more entries in the same `Promise.all` ‚Äî `loadCommitmentsWithDebt(now, tzOffsetMin)` and `loadGoalsWithPacing(now)` from `routes/goals.ts` ‚Äî feeding a `goals` block (**ACTIVE only**; the loader already settled the rest on this read) and a `commitments` block (every key, paused included). An **active** `replies` commitment's `dailyTarget` replaces `doctrine.replyTargetMin` as the quest's `repliesTarget` and an active `originals` one becomes `originalsTarget`; `replyQuota.target` stays the doctrine band (a personal minimum is not a redefinition of the 10‚Äì20/day doctrine). **`GET /brief` therefore WRITES goal statuses** ‚Äî opening Today is now what advances a finished goal. **A3.4:** one more $0 select in the same `Promise.all` ‚Äî the newest `audience_activity` row (full row = `ActiveTimesGrid` superset) ‚Äî passed to `annotateGaps` as an optional `audience`, so each gap gains `audienceScore: number|null` (display data for the TodayPlan row; **gap ordering is untouched** ‚Äî own-score-first, audience never reorders, ¬ß7.19/decision 10). **A3.5:** the today select includes `manual` (`['pending','manual','posted','failed']`) ‚Äî a manual slot is a filled slot; its anchor leaves the gap list. |
| `calendar.ts` | `POST /posts/scheduled` (URL guard on pending; optional validated `pillar` ‚Äî validates via `getActivePillars()`, so it **inherits the N.6 active-niche filter** for free, no code change), `POST /posts/threads`, `GET /posts/scheduled` (+filters), `GET/PATCH/DELETE /posts/scheduled/:id` (worker-owned statuses 409; PATCH `media_note`; GET returns thread siblings + `seededBy`). **GR.6:** the POST response gains `warnings: string[]` ‚Äî cluster (<`SCHEDULE_CLUSTER_MS` from another pending slot) + near-duplicate of a trailing-14d published original **or of another pending row**, all thresholds imported from `src/x/monitor.ts`. Computed in `scheduleWarnings(row)` **after the insert, inside a try/catch** and only for `pending` rows: **never a new 4xx** ‚Äî the URL guard stays the only content block on this route. **A3.5:** status value `manual` (create + PATCH; scheduledFor required like pending; **URL guard exempt** ‚Äî decision 5, no API call ever happens) + `POST /posts/scheduled/:id/mark-posted` (400/404/409 `not_manual`; flips to `posted`, never writes `posts_published`) + `manual_threads_unsupported` 400 on threads-create AND on PATCHing a thread member to manual (D117); create-status error now `create_status_must_be_draft_pending_or_manual` on the single route. **A3.7:** `scheduleWarnings` is now first-class over `manual` too ‚Äî it fires for `manual` rows AND counts manual neighbors (`inArray(['pending','manual'])`), wording `pending post`‚Üí`scheduled post` (D117 window opened once the Composer can create manual rows). |
| `metrics.ts` | `GET /metrics/replies`, `/metrics/posts`, `/metrics/account` (**S5.5** the Studio milestone card's client `api.metrics.account()` consumes this ‚Äî `{count,latest,series}`, `AccountSeriesPoint`), `/metrics/best-times` (`?tzOffsetMin=`, top gated at **`x.gates.bestTimeMinN`** ‚Äî UI.4, default 3, echoed as `minN`), `/metrics/pillars`, `/metrics/:tweetId`. |
| `posts.ts` | `POST /posts/reconcile` ‚Äî triggers the daily pass manually. |
| `analytics.ts` | **A3.2** ‚Äî audience Active-times captures, always mounted, **$0** (no X call, no LLM), static path only. `POST /analytics/active-times` (validate-then-insert append-only; bounds imported from `src/shared/activeTimes.ts` ‚Äî D114; grid values clamped [0,1] server-side; `captured_at` server-stamped) ‚Üí 201 `{capture}`; `GET /analytics/active-times` ‚Üí newest `{capture}`\|`{capture: null}`, `?history=n` (cap 30, 400 `invalid_history` on non-positive-int) ‚Üí `{count, captures}` newest-first (same-ms tie ‚Üí `id` desc). 400s: `invalid_body`/`invalid_metric`/`invalid_tz_offset_min`/`invalid_cols`/`invalid_rows`/`invalid_grid`. Consumers (A3.4 Composer blending, brief gaps) own the ¬ß7.19 ranking priority. |
| `pillars.ts` | `GET/POST /pillars`, `PATCH/DELETE /pillars/:slug` (last-active 409), `POST /pillars/draft` (proposal, runtime `llmConfigured()` check ‚Üí 503 `grok_not_configured` AI.6; **N.3** grounds on active niche persona+description; **AI.5** `loadPromptSafe('pillar-draft')` ‚Üí `template` into `buildPillarDraftInput`, `askLLM` w/ defaults low/700/0.7, body `provider` accepted, cache key `` `${prompt.cacheKey}:${slug}:${updatedAtMs}` `` ‚Äî `PILLAR_DRAFT_CACHE_KEY` gone). **N.6:** all reads scoped by `ownedByNiche(activeSlug)` = `niche = active.slug OR niche IS NULL` (legacy tolerance); POST stamps `niche = loadActiveNicheSafe().slug`; `getActivePillars()` falls back to `DEFAULT_PILLARS` **only when active niche is `builder`** (else `[]` ‚Äî the drafter refusal trigger); last-active 409 guard counts **within the active niche's set** (DELETE only guards when the target belongs to that set, so it can't false-fire on another niche's pillar). |
| `prompts.ts` | **AI.4** ‚Äî the prompt editor over `prompt_overrides` (always mounted next to `pillars` ‚Äî works with no LLM key). `GET /prompts` (list: key/name/description/required/`customized`=row-presence/`updatedAt`), `GET /prompts/:key` (body+`defaultBody`+customized+required, for diff/reset), `PATCH /prompts/:key {body}` (‚â§32KB ‚Üí 413 `body_too_large`; `validatePromptBody` ‚Üí 400 `missing_placeholder`+`missing`; upsert ‚Üí `{customized:true, unknownPlaceholders}`), `POST /prompts/:key/reset` (delete row ‚Üí `{customized:false}`), `POST /prompts/restore-defaults` (delete ALL ‚Üí `{restored:n}`); unknown key ‚Üí 404 `unknown_prompt`. Reuses the AI.3 registry; static `restore-defaults` + `:key/reset` param don't collide (¬ß7.20, different segment counts). |
| `niche.ts` | **N0.2** ‚Äî `GET /niche` (active niche + resolved doctrine, `DEFAULT_NICHE` fallback), `GET /niches` (active-first), `POST /niches` (created INACTIVE, 409 `slug_exists`), `PATCH /niches/:slug` (edit + doctrine; `active:true` ‚Üí atomic swap in a **sync** txn; `active:false` on the only active ‚Üí 409 `last_active_niche`), `DELETE /niches/:slug` (409 `niche_active` if active; owned pillars/channels keep their stamp). Validation mirrors pillars; doctrine rejects non-positive/non-numeric (no silent coerce). Always mounted, $0. **N0.8:** `POST /niche/draft` (the wizard) ‚Äî `{description ‚â§5000}` ‚Üí one `askGrok` structured-outputs call (effort low, `maxOutputTokens` 2500, cache key `stratus-niche-wizard`) ‚Üí parsed `NicheProposal` (never persisted). Description validated (400 `invalid_description`) BEFORE the runtime XAI key check (503 `grok_not_configured`) so the $0 guards are testable without a key; the paid call is last (¬ß7.4). `POST /niche/draft` ‚âÝ `POST /niches` ‚Äî no `:slug` collision. |
| `me.ts` | **ME.2** ‚Äî `GET /me?kind=&active=` (entries each w/ server-computed `inWindow` via `isEntryInWindow`; goals each w/ `progress`), `POST/PATCH/DELETE /me/entries[/:id]` (kind/text‚â§1000/happenedAt-ISO/pinned/active; per-field 400 codes), `POST/PATCH/DELETE /me/goals[/:id]` (label/kind/target>0/unit/deadline/currentValue/status), `GET /me/context?mode=post\|reply` ‚Üí `{mode, block\|null}` (the exact injected block, ¬ß7.18). Exports **`loadMeContextSafe(mode)`** ‚Äî active entries + active goals + latest `account_snapshots` followers ‚Üí `selectEntriesForPrompt`/`resolveGoals` ‚Üí render; null on empty OR any error (¬ß7.8, never throws). Always mounted, $0 (pure SQL). Static `/me` prefix + `:id` params shadow nothing (¬ß7.20). **ME.3** consumes `loadMeContextSafe` in `drafter.ts` (post) + `routes/replies.ts` (single stamps `ctx.me`, batch passes `meBrief`). |
| `drafter.ts` | `POST /posts/draft` (3 register-distinct drafts ‚Üí `status='draft'` rows), `POST /posts/reup` (self-quote drafts; ownership via posts_published), **`POST /posts/draft-thread`** (**AI.7** ‚Äî `{idea?,ideaId?,pillar?,tweetCount?,model?,provider?,reasoningEffort?}` ‚Üí one structured-outputs call via `loadPromptSafe('thread')` + `buildThreadDraftInput`/`buildThreadDraftSchema` ‚Üí `insertThreadDraft` lands a `status='draft'` head + `status='segment'` tails sharing a threadId, `source='drafter'`; **one auto-regenerate** if a segment >280 chars (nudge names them, still-long ‚Üí 502 `thread_invalid`); `tweetCount` non-int ‚Üí 400 `invalid_tweet_count`, clamp 3‚Äì8; `consumeIdeaSafe` after insert; URL allowed in drafts. `insertThreadDraft(pillar,tweets,ideaId?)` exported for the route test), **`POST /posts/rewrite`** (**AI.8** ‚Äî `{text [1‚Äì2000], instruction? [‚â§500], model?, provider?}` ‚Üí inline validation [`invalid_body`/`invalid_text`/`invalid_instruction`/`invalid_model`/`invalid_provider`, all pre-spend] ‚Üí `loadPromptSafe('rewrite')` + `buildRewriteInput` ‚Üí `askLLM` [defaults 0.7/900/low, cache key = bare `prompt.cacheKey`] ‚Üí **no DB rows**; `parseRewrite` null ‚Üí 502 `rewrite_parse_error`, `[]` ‚Üí 502 `rewrite_invalid`; over-long variants dropped, never truncated). LLM-gated mount (**AI.6** `llmConfigured()`). **N.3:** `generateAndInsert` loads `loadActiveNicheSafe()`, passes persona/beliefs, cache key `` `${PROMPT_CACHE_KEY}:${slug}:${updatedAtMs}` ``. **N.6:** both routes refuse `409 {error:'no_pillars_for_niche', niche}` when `getActivePillars()` is `[]` (a custom niche with no active pillars) ‚Äî BEFORE any Grok spend (¬ß7.4). `POST /pillars/draft` deliberately does NOT refuse (empty `existing` is how the first pillar is made). **AI.3:** the prompt comes from `loadPromptSafe('post')` (`template` into `buildPostDraftInput`), cache key `` `${prompt.cacheKey}:${slug}:${updatedAtMs}` `` (static `PROMPT_CACHE_KEY` gone). **AI.5:** `generateAndInsert` calls `askLLM` (defaults temp 0.7/600/low); `parseCommon` accepts `provider` (400 `invalid_provider`) and returns `reasoningEffort` only when body-supplied (house default rides the defaults tier); errors via `llmErrorPayload`. |
| `replies.ts` | `POST /replies/generate` (band gate 422 BEFORE spend ‚Üí relationship+guidance stamp ‚Üí 3 variants, `MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS=520` ‚Üí specificity gate w/ one auto-regen), `POST /replies/generate-batch` (‚â§25, **3 variants/post RU.3**, `maxOutputTokens=min(9000,200+n*420)`, response items `{tweetId,text,angle,variants}` primary=variants[0], no DB rows, persists `radar_drafts`), `GET /replies`, `/replies/outcomes` (¬ß6.2 join), `/replies/default-prompt`, `GET/PATCH/DELETE /replies/:id` (PATCH‚Üíposted = paste time, logs my_reply, backfills postedTweetId). | `harvest.ts` | `POST /harvest/runs`, `POST /harvest/rows` (‚â§500; replies-mode reconcile ‚Üí backfills draft `postedTweetId`), `GET /harvest/runs`. **HV.1** `POST /harvest/passive` (‚â§100/batch, **$0**, zero schema change): ambient home-timeline rows into the SAME `harvest_rows`, discriminated by `mode='timeline'` and hung off ONE server-created run per UTC day (`{handle:'timeline', mode:'timeline', scope:'passive'}`) ‚Äî `MODES` deliberately still excludes `'timeline'`, so `POST /harvest/runs` keeps rejecting it and clients can never forge a passive run (decision 7). Gates in order: lazy 60d retention prune (`mode='timeline'` only ‚Äî a hand-run harvest of the same age survives) ‚Üí find-or-create today's run (`createdAt >= utcDayStart(now)`) ‚Üí in-batch dedupe by tweetId + 30-min recapture gate (both counted as `skippedRecent`; served by `harvest_rows_tweet_captured_idx`) ‚Üí daily cap 2000 (`skippedCap`) ‚Üí one sync txn insert + `rowCount` bump. Always `201 {runId, inserted, skippedRecent, skippedCap}`. Band is NEVER stored (¬ß7.12 ‚Äî recomputable from views/comments/tweetTime/capturedAt/text); **no person events** (decision 6 ‚Äî timeline exposure is not an interest signal; affinity is the read-time bridge in HV.4). Pure exported `utcDayStart(now)`. **HV.4** `GET /harvest/affinity?days=&limit=&minDays=` (**$0**, static path ‚Äî the router still has no `:param` route, so ¬ß7.20 is a "keep it that way" note, not a live trap) ‚Üí `{days, minDays, authors: AffinityAuthor[]}` where `AffinityAuthor = {handle, distinctDays, sightings, lastSeenAt (ISO), avgViews (rounded), stage: Stage|null, inRoster}`. ONE grouped select over `harvest_rows` **filtered `mode='timeline'`** + `capturedAt >= now‚àídays`, grouped by handle, `having distinctDays >= minDays`, ordered **distinctDays desc then sightings desc** (a viral thread re-scrolled 20√ó in one afternoon is not affinity), limit. Distinct days = `count(distinct strftime('%Y-%m-%d', captured_at/1000, 'unixepoch'))` ‚Äî **UTC**, matching `utcDayStart` and the panel's `passiveRowsToday`. The `people`/`voice_authors` join happens **in TS** off the ‚â§`limit` handles (never `in ()` ‚Äî early return when the group-by is empty); handles are lowercased on every side so no `lower()` wrapper is needed. `stage` is null unless a NON-retired people row exists, but `inRoster` counts retired rows too ‚Äî a person you deliberately retired is known, not a fresh candidate to nag about. Params via the shared `intParam` helper: absent ‚Üí default, out of range ‚Üí **clamped** (days 7‚Äì90, limit 1‚Äì50, minDays ‚â•1), non-positive-integer ‚Üí **400** `invalid_days`/`invalid_limit`/`invalid_min_days`. Own tweets are NOT filtered out (decision 8 ‚Äî filtering is analysis-time). |
| `following.ts` | **GR.1** ‚Äî the $0 following ledger (always mounted; nothing in the file can reach `xFetch`, and unfollowing stays a manual act in the X app). `POST /following/runs` `{}` ‚Üí 201 run row. `POST /following/rows` `{runId, rows[‚â§500], done?}` ‚Üí 201 `{runId, received, applied, inserted, updated, rowsSeen, complete, reconcile}`: in-batch dedupe by handle (**first occurrence wins** ‚Äî the page renders top-down, so the earliest sighting carries the truest `list_position`), then ONE sync txn (¬ß7.13) inserting fresh handles and updating known ones. **Upsert rules:** `first_seen_at` fill-only; `follows_back` always refreshed; a field the scrape didn't report (`displayName`/`listPosition` null) is left alone, never nulled (¬ß7.11); a `confirmed`/`gone` row seen again is **revived to `active`** (presence is ground truth ‚Äî D99a) but keeps its `first_seen_at` and its `unfollow_marked_at`. **Reconcile fires only on `done:true` AND `rowsSeen > 0`** ‚Äî "unseen" is `last_run_id != runId` (every batch stamps it, so no in-memory set): unseen `active|queued`‚Üí`gone`, unseen `done`‚Üí`confirmed`, **seen `done`‚Üí`queued`** (the one reverse edge: the tick didn't take). A run closed with 0 rows is stamped `completed_at` but **`complete` stays false** (D99b) so it neither reconciles nor counts as a fresh sync. Errors: 400 `invalid_body`/`invalid_run_id`/`invalid_done`/`rows_required` (empty rows are legal ONLY with `done:true` ‚Äî D99c)/`too_many_rows`/indexed `invalid_row`/`invalid_handle`/`invalid_display_name`/`invalid_follows_back`/`invalid_list_position`, 404 `run_not_found`, 409 `run_already_complete`. `GET /following?status=&q=&limit=` ‚Üí `{count, total, lastCompleteRunAt, following}` ‚Äî `q` is `instr()` not LIKE (a handle legitimately contains `_`, which LIKE reads as a wildcard). `PATCH /following/:handle` `{status:'done'}` (**only** from `queued`, stamps `unfollow_marked_at`; anything else 409 `invalid_transition`, unknown status 400, **not idempotent** ‚Äî re-ticking a `done` row 409s) and/or `{keep}` (an independent pin that moves NO status ‚Äî the queue filters kept rows out of the batch itself). 400 `empty_patch`/`invalid_keep`, 404 `not_found`. **`GET /following/queue` (GR.3) is registered ABOVE `/following/:handle`** (¬ß7.20) ‚Üí `{batch:[{handle, displayName, firstSeenAt, url}], eligibleTotal, releasedNow, windowUsed, windowCap, dailyUsed, dailyCeiling, lastCompleteRunAt}`. All read-time (¬ß7.12): loads active+queued rows, assembles the whitelist (people stage mutual/ally non-retired + `loadTargetHandles()`; `keep` is a column, enforced in the pure fns), reads trailing-24h `unfollow_marked_at` for the budget, then in ONE sync txn flips released `active‚Üíqueued` and revoked `queued‚Üíactive`. **Idempotent:** the batch tops up to `budget` total, so a re-read with held ‚â• budget releases nothing; already-queued rows re-list until ticked `done`. Pure logic in `connections.ts` (¬ß3.3). |
