`status:'published'` stamps `publishedAt` **only on entry** (published‚Üídraft keeps it as history; a re-publish re-stamps), `publishedUrl` ‚â§400; a **`discarded` row is frozen** ‚Äî the only accepted edit is a bare `{status:'draft'}` revive, anything else ‚Üí **409 `discarded_locked`** (dm_drafts terminal-status precedent). `DELETE /articles/:id` hard-deletes (204). 400s: `invalid_id`/`invalid_body`/`invalid_title`/`invalid_subtitle`/`invalid_body_md`/`invalid_pillar`/`invalid_outline`/`invalid_published_url`/`invalid_status`/`invalid_limit`/`empty_patch`; 404 `not_found`. **A3.12: `POST /articles/:id/assist {mode:outline\|section\|polish\|full, idea?, heading?, selection?}`** ‚Äî the Grok writing assist (one `askLLM` call, D5-gated). $0 refusal ladder `invalid_id`/`invalid_body`/`invalid_mode` ‚Üí per-mode seed 400 (`idea_required`/`heading_required`/`selection_required`) ‚Üí 404 ‚Üí **409 `discarded_locked`** (a discarded article is frozen ‚Äî revive first) ‚Üí **503 `grok_not_configured`** (`!llmConfigured()`) ‚Üí $0 loaders (`getActivePillars`/`topWinners`/`loadPostGuidanceSafe`) ‚Üí `askLLM(loadPromptSafe('article'), low/1200 tok [3000 for full]/0.7, prompt.cacheKey)`; `assist_failed` 502 / `assist_parse_error` 502. Returns `{mode, proposal, persisted, costUsd, model, requestId}`. **Only `outline` writes** (persists `articles.outline`, fills default title/subtitle); section/polish/full return text the editor inserts. Reuses this file's `UUID_RE`/`parseNullableText`/`DEFAULT_TITLE` ‚Äî the assist route‚Üíroute-imports `topWinners` (drafter.ts) + `loadPostGuidanceSafe` (playbook.ts) with no cycle. |
| `channels.ts` | `GET/POST /channels`, `GET /channels/:slug` (the aggregate room), `PATCH/DELETE /channels/:slug`. **N.6:** `GET /channels` scoped by `ownedByNiche(activeSlug)` (`niche = active.slug OR NULL`); POST stamps `niche = loadActiveNicheSafe().slug`; the `:slug` room 404s when the channel belongs to a non-active niche (NULL-niche legacy rows stay visible); PATCH/DELETE untouched (slug-addressed). Extension `ChannelTags` + content-script chips inherit the filter with zero client change. |
| `playbook.ts` | `GET /playbook?minN=`, `POST /playbook/extract-winners` (‚â§20 winners/call, runtime `llmConfigured()` check ‚Üí 503 `grok_not_configured` AI.6; **AI.5** shares `loadPromptSafe('voice-extract')` + `renderPrompt` with voiceExtract's path, `askLLM`, body `provider` accepted). Loaders + `loadReplyGuidanceSafe`/`loadPostGuidanceSafe` (always the CONFIGURED gate ‚Äî **UI.4**: `?minN=` overrides per read, but the baseline for the page AND the injected guidance is `x.gates.minCellN`, default 20) + exported `loadFollowersByHandle`. **ME.5:** `ReplyRow.hasMe` (from `ctx.me`) feeds `meEffectiveness` in the payload ‚Äî no new query, same reply rows as relationship lift. **RU.9:** `loadOriginRows` selects `replyDrafts.source` alongside `postedTweetId` and builds the `postedTweetId‚Üísource` map fed to `classifyReplyOrigin` (exact radar attribution, text-match only as the no-draft-link fallback). **RL.7:** one more unwindowed select ‚Äî every `reply_list_uses.renderedText` normalized into a `Set` (empty strings skipped) ‚Äî feeds the `canned` bucket; the table is FK-free so a deleted list never erases its attribution. **HV.5:** `loadTimelineFunnel(minN)` ‚Üí `timelineFunnel` in the payload ‚Äî ONE grouped select over `harvest_rows` **filtered `mode='timeline'`** + `capturedAt >= now‚àí30d`, `min(captured_at)` with bare columns (SQLite's documented first-sighting form: with exactly one min/max aggregate every bare column comes from the matching row) `group by tweet_id`, then the posted-`reply_drafts.sourceTweetId` set intersected against it. Window is 30d (shorter than the 60d passive retention on purpose) and **unlimited by design** ‚Äî volume is structurally bounded by HV.1's 2,000-rows/day cap, and a `limit` would truncate the denominator. $0. |
| `digest.ts` | `GET /digest?week=&tzOffsetMin=&refresh=&factsOnly=` (cached per week; degrades to facts on LLM failure). **ME.5:** facts carry `goals` ‚Äî `loadGoals(now)` = active `me_goals` √ó latest `account_snapshots` followers via `resolveGoals`, null when none. **AI.6:** `loadPromptSafe('digest')` ‚Üí `buildDigestInput(facts, prompt.body)` + `askLLM` (defaults low/700/0.7, `prompt.cacheKey` replaces the static `stratus-digest`); the no-key degrade + catch classify to `llm_not_configured`/`grok_<status>`/`openrouter_<status>`/`llm_parse_error`/`llm_failed` (gate = `llmConfigured()`; the extension `Digest.tsx` matcher moved to `llm_not_configured`). **GR.9:** `loadFacts(start, end, weekKey, tzOffsetMin, now)` also assembles the scorecard inputs ‚Äî `daysWithOriginal` = distinct `localDayKey(postedAt, tz)` over the week's non-reply `posts_published` (`postedAt` added to that select, never reaching the facts JSON), `daysInWeek` = 7 once the week is over else the elapsed days, `repliesTargetWeek` = the ACTIVE `replies` commitment's `dailyTarget` else `doctrine.replyTargetMin`, **√ó daysInWeek** (same resolution as GR.8's quests; the debt half of `loadCommitmentsWithDebt` is unused here ‚Äî the loader is imported so "which commitment is active" has one reading), `goalVerdicts` = active goals off **`loadGoalsWithPacing`**, and `loadPrevScore(weekKey)` reads last week's cached `digests.facts.scorecard.score` (missing/ungraded ‚Üí null delta, never a comparison against 0). **Consequence: generating a digest now WRITES** (the goals loader's `active‚Üíachieved|missed` flip) ‚Äî the fifth read-that-writes after `/radar/drafts`, `/following/queue`, `/x/goals` and `/x/brief`; the cache path returns before it, so re-opening Sunday's digest doesn't re-flip, but `x_digest` (factsOnly) does. |
| `brief`/`streaks` | streak upsert happens inside `GET /brief` (idempotent per local day). |
| `images.ts` | `POST /images/generate` (n‚â§2; HARD daily budget `x.budgets.imageDailyUsd` read per call ‚Üí 429 before spend, `0` disables generation; returns data: URLs). |
| `assets.ts` | `POST /assets` (‚â§2MB), `GET /assets` (metadata only), `GET /assets/:id/png` (bytes), `DELETE /assets/:id`. |
| `data.ts` | `GET /data/tables`, `GET /data/:table`, `POST /data/query` ‚Äî S1 read-only; plus the `explorer` router mounted at root **outside bearer** (data-free shells, ¬ß7.21): `GET /explorer` (S1) and **A3.13** `GET /writer` (the Writer page ‚Äî both lazy `Bun.file`-cache `public/*.html`; adding `/writer` needed no `index.ts` change, the router was already `app.route('/', explorer)`). |
| `settings.ts` | UI.1 (mounted next to `data`): `GET /settings` (groups + value + isDefault), `GET /settings/values?scope=mirrored` (flat mirror payload), `PATCH /settings` (per-key validated, all-or-nothing ‚Üí 400 `unknown_setting`/`invalid_setting_value`), `POST /settings/reset` (`{keys?,group?}`). Always mounted, $0; **landed inert ‚Äî no store consumer yet** (UI.2‚Äì7 wire them). |

Shared/other: `GET /healthz` (public), `GET/cost/today`, `GET /cost/daily`, `POST /grok/ask`, `POST /mcp` (JSON-RPC; GET/DELETE‚Üí405).

## 4. Database ‚Äî 40 tables

`src/db/shared-schema.ts`: **cost_events** (platform-tagged spend ledger) ¬∑ **app_settings** (UI.1 ‚Äî settings overrides; key PK, JSON value, `updatedAt`; only overridden keys get a row).

`src/x/db/schema.ts` (schema line numbers as of stamp):

| Table | Purpose / notes |
|---|---|
| `tokens` (L14) | Single row `id='default'` OAuth tokens. Excluded from explorer/MCP entirely. |
| `contentPillars` (L33) | Editable pillars; seed INSERT lives in migration 0000. Never let the active set go empty (409 guards). **N0.1** adds nullable `niche` (backfilled `'builder'`, migration 0015). |
| `channels` (L54) | C8 topic rooms: slug PK, keywords JSON, optional pillar link (not FK-validated). **N0.1** adds nullable `niche` (backfilled `'builder'`). |
| `niches` (L70) | **N0.1** ‚Äî first-class identity container: slug PK, `persona`/`beliefs`/`replyPersona` (prompt-grounding, lifted verbatim from post ¬ß1/¬ß5 + reply "Who I am"), `description`, `doctrine` JSON (null=defaults), `active` (exactly one, v1). Seeded `builder` mirroring `DEFAULT_NICHE` byte-for-byte (migration 0015). **INERT until N0.3/N0.4/N0.5** wire consumers. |
| `mediaAssets` (L77) | S4 Studio PNGs as BLOBs (kind, prompt, w/h, usedOnTweetId). `assets.ts` `ASSET_KINDS` whitelist widened (**S5.5**) to all S5 template ids ‚Äî `quote/stat/banner/pfp/milestone/streak/code/thread/list/chart/background/other`; unknown ‚Üí `'other'`. |
| `scheduledPosts` (L94) | Calendar. status `draft\|pending\|manual\|publishing\|posted\|failed\|cancelled\|segment`; `thread_id`, `position`, `quote_tweet_id`, `pillar`, `register`, `media_note`, `source`. `publishing`/`posted` worker-owned. **A3.5** `manual` = user pastes at the slot; unclaimable (publisher claims `pending` only), ‚Üí `posted` via mark-posted or the A3.6 reconcile; never on thread rows. |
| `postsPublished` (L139) | Everything actually posted (incl. app-made): `in_reply_to_tweet_id`, `conversation_id`, `has_media` (null=unknown, never "no"). |
| `metricsSnapshots` (L164) | Once-only snapshots; `age_at_snapshot_min`; joined newest-first-wins everywhere. |
| `postTemplates` (L189) | C4 extracted winner structures (hook/skeleton/device, lowercased keys). |
| `accountSnapshots` (L205) | Daily getMe KPI, 1/UTC-day, + `pinned_tweet_id` (S0.9). Latest row = "my size" for banding. |
| `voiceAuthors` (L225) / `voiceAuthorSnapshots` (L253) / `voiceTweets` (L268) | Swipe file (DOM-scraped, $0): profile + follower series (append per enrich) + tweets (`scraped_html`, template columns from ¬ß8.3, `tags`). |
| `replyDrafts` (L301) | Grok reply drafts: `variants` JSON, `source` (RU.2 ‚Äî `'reply_master'\|'radar'`, null=legacy), `contextSnapshot` (records exactly what the model saw ‚Äî signals, relationship, guidance), `postedTweetId` (the outcome join key), `idea`, `pillar`. `updatedAt` of posted flip = paste time. |
| `radarDrafts` (L357) | C0 persisted batch replies; status `ready\|clicked\|expired` ratchet; 48h lazy expiry; `tags`; RU.2 adds `variants` JSON, `model`, `reply_draft_id` (soft link, no FK); **RU.3** `buildRadarDraftRows` stores `r.variants` from the batch (null when a CLI/smoke caller passes only the primary text/angle); **RU.5** `POST ‚Ä¶/confirm` writes `reply_draft_id` + ratchets status‚Üí`clicked` when a draft is promoted to a `reply_drafts` row; **RU.8** the `band` column now also stores `'manual'` (a ‚äï pinned tweet), coerced away from the confirmed reply snapshot's classifier signals. |
| `people` (L397) / `personEvents` (L428) / `personSnapshots` (L449) | C1 CRM: handle PK + stage + watermarks; append-only timeline (**deterministic ids** `type:ref_table:ref_id`, INSERT OR IGNORE); ambient follower series (C6 hover, once/day gates). **NT.2 (comment-only, no migration):** `type` is free text ‚Äî its comment now lists `their_like`/`their_repost`/`their_follow`; `source` lists `hover`/`launch`/`notification` (the old list was already stale). |
| `ideas` (L470) | C6 Idea Inbox: status `open\|consumed\|discarded`, consume provenance (`consumed_by_table/-id` restricted to reply_drafts/scheduled_posts). |
| `followupSnoozes` (L496) | item_key `kind:handle` or `reup:<tweetId>`. |
| `streaks` (L509) | Local-day PK diary (C9); upserted by brief reads. |
| `digests` (L522) | Weekly digest cache (week_key PK). |
| `mentions` (L542) | Inbox; **max stored tweet_id IS the since_id checkpoint** ‚Äî never insert non-API ids; status flow + `answered_draft_id`. **Two DOM surfaces route around this trap:** C7 `launch.ts` (early repliers ‚Üí person events only) and NT.5's notifications surface (reads mention rows for parent context, writes none ‚Äî the freshness gap is closed by the human sync chip, not by inserting scraped ids). |
| `conversationMeta` (L568) | C2 snooze/read/mute per conversation_id. |
| `harvestRuns` (L630) / `harvestRows` (L643) | DOM harvest; repeated captures on purpose (longitudinal series); content-shape columns; index `(tweet_id, captured_at)`. **HV.1 added NO column and NO migration** ‚Äî `mode`/`scope` are free-text, so passive rows are `mode='timeline'` + `scope='passive'` on existing fields (orig\*/`group_position`/`matched_draft_id` null). The only other reader, `scripts/backfill-people.ts`, filters `mode='replies'`, so passive rows can't pollute it ‚Äî **any new consumer MUST filter on `mode`**. Readers of the `mode='timeline'` corpus so far: `GET /harvest/affinity` (HV.4) and `loadTimelineFunnel` in `routes/playbook.ts` (HV.5). |
| `meEntries` (L689) | **ME.1** Me profile: `kind` (fact/event/emotion/note), `text`, `happened_at` (null=undated ‚Üí created_at drives windows), `pinned`/`active`. No seed (empty = byte-identical prompts). |
| `meGoals` (L711) | **ME.1** Measurable goals, extended by **GR.7 (D4 ‚Äî one goals system, no second table)**: `kind` is now a 5-union (`followers`/`mrr`/`custom` + the counted `posted_replies`/`originals`), `status` gained `missed`, and `baseline_value`/`baseline_at` record where the goal started (null on pre-GR.7 rows ‚Üí readers fall back to `created_at`). `current_value` stays the manual column for mrr/custom; followers reads `account_snapshots`; the counted kinds are tallied from their own baseline and are the only kinds NOT injected into the me-block. |
| `commitments` (L746) | **GR.7** Daily minimums I hold myself to: `key` PK (`replies`/`originals`), `daily_target`, `active`, `active_since`, `updated_at`. **No seed** ‚Äî an absent row means no commitment and the quest targets fall back to the doctrine defaults. `active_since` is stamped at creation and on re-activation only (never on a target edit), because it is the day the promise starts and `commitmentDebt` counts from it. |
| `replyLists` (L757) / `replyListItems` (L777) / `replyListUses` (L809) | **RL.2** Canned reply lists: list (`humanizer` JSON, null = engine defaults, stored NORMALIZED through `parseHumanizerConfig`) ‚Üí items (template `text`, `enabled`, `source` manual/ai, **`last_used_at`/`use_count` = the server-side anti-repeat state**, FK `list_id` **ON DELETE CASCADE**, index `(list_id, last_used_at)` = exactly what `pickItem`'s recency window reads) ‚Üí uses (the audit log AND the Playbook `canned` measurement hook via a normalized `rendered_text` match; **deliberately NOT FK'd** so the history outlives an edited-away item or a deleted list; index `(used_at)`). Migration 0018, DDL-only, no seed. |
| `followingRuns` (L836) / `following` (L862) | **GR.1** Following ledger from ONE $0 DOM scrape of my own `/following` page (X renders a "Follows you" badge per row, so one pass yields both sides ‚Äî no API sync, no `follows.write` scope). Run: `started_at`/`completed_at`/`rows_seen`/**`complete`** ‚Äî the trust flag, since only a run that walked the WHOLE list may conclude anything from a handle's absence. Ledger: handle PK (lowercased), `display_name`, `follows_back` (notNull ‚Äî the badge's absence IS the "no", there is no third state), `list_position` (render order ‚âà follow recency, a tie-break not a date), `first_seen_at` **fill-only** (the follow-date proxy ¬ß7.11 ‚Äî `followed_at` deliberately doesn't exist), `last_seen_at`, `last_run_id` FK, `status` (active\|queued\|done\|confirmed\|gone), `keep` (manual never-suggest pin), `unfollow_marked_at` (**never cleared** ‚Äî the 6h/24h churn budgets count marks in a trailing window). Index `(status, first_seen_at)` = exactly GR.3's eligibility query. |
| `audienceActivity` (L929) | **A3.2** Audience Active-times heatmap captures ($0 DOM scrape of X Analytics, A3.3 will write them): `captured_at` (server-stamped, indexed), `metric` (the analytics dropdown, free text), `tz_offset_min` (grid is viewer-local wall-clock), `cols`/`rows`, `grid` JSON `number[cols][rows]` 0..1 col 0 = Monday. **Append-only** ‚Äî repeated captures = longitudinal series; newest row = "current" for A3.4's slot blending. Presence data, never ¬ß7.19-gated at storage; own gated best-time cells always outrank it in consumers. |
| `dmDrafts` (L951) | **A3.9** Grounded outbound DM drafts (`POST /x/dms/draft`): `id` uuid, `handle` (FK ‚Üí `people.handle`, indexed with `created_at`), `text`, `purpose?`, `status` (`draft`\|`sent`\|`discarded`, default draft), `grounding` JSON `{block, idea}` (¬ß7.16 ‚Äî exactly what the model saw), `cost_usd?`, `created/updated/sent_at`. Written only by `routes/dms.ts`; `sent` is terminal and logs a `manual_dm_logged` person event. |
| `articles` (L987) | **A3.11** Long-form Markdown originals for the `/writer` page (`routes/articles.ts`): `id` uuid, `title` (notNull, defaults `'Untitled'` at the route), `subtitle?`, `body_md` (notNull default `''`), `pillar?` (validated against active slugs at write time, stored free-text), `status` (`draft`\|`published`\|`discarded`, default draft), `outline` JSON (shape owned by the A3.12 assist), `published_url?` (‚â§400), `published_at?`, `created/updated_at`. Index `(status, updated_at)` = exactly the list query. No API article publish exists ‚Äî posting is a manual "Copy for X", so no URL surcharge ever applies. `published_at` stamps only on the draft‚Üípublished transition; a `discarded` row is frozen except a bare revive to draft. |
| `promptOverrides` (L748) | **AI.3** Editable-prompt OVERRIDE ROWS ONLY (key = registry `PromptKey`, body, updatedAt). Row absent = the shipped default in `prompts/registry.ts` applies; restore = DELETE; `customized` = row presence. No seed by design (a later-deploy default improvement applies unless overridden). Explorer/MCP-visible ‚Äî never store secrets. |

Migrations `0000`‚Äì`0023` (latest: `0023_slimy_night_thrasher` A3.11 ‚Äî 1 CREATE TABLE (`articles`) + 1 index (`articles_status_updated_idx`), DDL-only, no seed, no FK, nothing touched on existing tables. `0022_chilly_tomas` A3.9 ‚Äî 1 CREATE TABLE (`dm_drafts`) + FK to `people.handle` + 1 index, DDL-only, no seed. `0021_square_iron_monger` A3.2 ‚Äî 1 CREATE TABLE (`audience_activity`) + 1 index, DDL-only, no seed. `0020_tidy_thunderbolts` GR.7 ‚Äî 1 CREATE TABLE (`commitments`) + 2 nullable `me_goals` ADD COLUMNs, DDL-only, no seed; nullable adds are the only safe way to widen a live table on SQLite. `0019_messy_blue_shield` GR.1 `following`+`following_runs` ‚Äî 2 CREATE TABLEs + 1 index, DDL-only, no seed, nothing touched on existing tables. `following` is created BEFORE the `following_runs` it FKs to; SQLite resolves FK targets at DML time, not CREATE time, so the order is harmless. `0018_flimsy_captain_universe` RL.2 `reply_lists`+`reply_list_items`+`reply_list_uses` ‚Äî 3 CREATE TABLEs + 2 indexes, DDL-only, no seed, nothing touched on existing tables; `0013` app_settings, `0014` RU.2 reply `source` + radar `variants`/`model`/`reply_draft_id`, `0015` N0.1 `niches` table + seed INSERT + nullable `niche` on content_pillars/channels + `UPDATE ‚Ä¶ SET niche='builder'` backfills ‚Äî the seed/backfill DML was hand-appended after generate, `0016_high_miek` ME.1 `me_entries`+`me_goals` ‚Äî DDL-only, no seed, `0017_misty_zeigeist` AI.3 `prompt_overrides` ‚Äî single CREATE TABLE, no seed by design). Workflow: edit schema ‚Üí `bun run db:generate` ‚Üí **inspect the SQL** (drizzle drops seed INSERTs; keep them idempotent) ‚Üí boot/`deploy.sh` migrates. (biome now ignores `src/db/migrations` ‚Äî UI.1, D11/D13.)

## 5. Extension ‚Äî `extension/` (own package.json, Vite + React, MV3)

**Build:** two passes (`vite.config.ts`) ‚Äî content script first as self-contained **IIFE** (`content.js`; classic script, no imports allowed), then side panel + background as ES modules. Shared modules used by content.ts get inlined. Out-of-tree server modules reach the extension via **re-export shims**: `extension/src/replyBand.ts` ‚Üí `src/shared/replyBand.ts`, `extension/src/channelSuggest.ts` ‚Üí `src/shared/channelSuggest.ts`, `extension/src/shared/activeTimes.ts` ‚Üí `src/shared/activeTimes.ts` (A3.1 ‚Äî this one also ADDS the DOM extractor on top of the re-export; tsconfig lists all three in `include`).

**Manifest:** side panel + background service worker + content script on x.com/twitter.com. Permissions: sidePanel, storage, clipboardWrite/Read, contextMenus, alarms, notifications.

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `src/background.ts` | Service worker. **Single writer of all `chrome.storage.session` state** (radar ring buffer cap 100 + dismissed cap 500, launch room state), writes serialized via promise chain. One HTTP transport: `ApiRequest` message channel ‚Äî the only Authorization-header owner (incl. `binary` for asset blobs). Rankmap cache (10min TTL, S0.3). C7 launch alarms (`chrome.alarms`, +90s grace, liveness verify, notification). **A3.8 manual-post reminders** (own `manualChain`/`enqueueManual` ‚Äî a distinct session-key family): a sibling `syncManualAlarms()` alongside `syncLaunchAlarms()` at all three launch triggers fetches `?status=manual&from=now‚àí30min&to=now+24h` ‚Üí `computeManualAlarms` ‚Üí one `stratus-manual:<id>` alarm AT `scheduledFor` (no grace/retry); `parseManualAlarm` dispatches in `onAlarm` BEFORE `parseLaunchAlarm`; `handleManualFire` re-GETs the row and, only if still `manual`, `mergeManualDue`-writes the `manual:due` entry (dedup by postId, cap 5) + fires a `stratus-manual-note:<id>` notification (`manualNotificationText`); `stratus/manual-dismiss {postId}`‚Üí`dismissManualDue`; the notification-click handler opens the panel for the manual prefix too. Ideas context menu. **RU.6** `stratus/radar-confirm` handler ‚Üí `confirmDraft(tweetId)` POSTs `/x/radar/drafts/:id/confirm` (best-effort ¬ß7.8; ignores `unconfigured`) then `stampDraftId` writes the returned reply_drafts `id` onto the sighting (single writer, markClicked pattern). **RU.7** `stratus/radar-variants-get`‚Üí`getVariants` (session buffer `isReplyVariants(hit.variants)` first, else `GET /x/radar/drafts?tweetId=` ‚Üí newest row's `.drafts[0]`, variants ?? `[{text:replyText, angle}]`) returns `{variants, draftId}|null`; `stratus/radar-variant-pasted`‚Üí`pasteVariant` POSTs the idempotent confirm (covers deep links) then PATCHes `/x/replies/:id {status:'posted', replyTextEdited?}` ‚Äî the confirm response IS the reply_drafts row so its `replyText` is the primary (chosen text ‚âÝ primary ‚Üí `replyTextEdited`); best-effort ¬ß7.8, warn-only. **AX.6** `stratus/open-person`‚Üí`chrome.sidePanel.open({tabId: sender.tab?.id})` [best-effort user-gesture, one-hop] + writes the `stratus:openPerson` session handoff key `{handle, at}` via its own `enqueueOpenPerson` chain [single writer]; `stratus/open-person-clear`‚Üíremoves the key. **NT.4** notifications context: `NOTIF_CONTEXT_TTL_MS`=5min + `notifContext`/`notifContextAt`/`notifContextInflight` (rankmap-cache idiom; only a successful pull advances the stamp) ‚Äî `refreshNotifContext()` GETs `/x/mentions?limit=200` and maps rows to `{parentText, status}` by reply `tweetId`; `stratus/notif-context`‚Üí`notifContextPayload(force)` awaits `refreshNotifContext`+`refreshRankMap` in parallel (both TTL-guarded no-ops) ‚Üí `{ok:true, mentions, rankMap}`, and on `force` it drains any in-flight refresh THEN invalidates (a sync click must not be answered by a pull that started before it). **Always `ok:true`** ‚Äî every failure path degrades to the last-good/empty map. |
| `src/content.ts` | On-page: reply-band **border/dim** (`readTweetSignals`; **AX.3** the green stats *badge* is gone ‚Äî border/dim + `recordRadarSighting` byte-identical, radar stream untouched) + **AX.3 person chips** (`applyPersonChips(article, glance)` from `scan` decorates the `[data-testid="User-Name"]` line via `buildPersonChips` over a `GET /people/glance` `GLANCE_TTL_MS` module cache [channels pattern; sync `getGlanceMap`‚Üíbg `refreshGlanceMap`, `unconfigured` silent], recompute-per-scan `data-handle`+`data-sig` skip-guard, chip `<button>`s carry `data-tone`/`data-handle`, **AX.6** click ‚Üí `sendOpenPerson(handle)` [preventDefault+stopPropagation so X never navigates];
