**S5.8** +`chart`, `supportsAiBackground:false`), `TEMPLATES` metadata (`id`/`label`/`size {w,h}`/`supportsAiBackground`), `templateMeta`/`supportsAiBackground` helpers, `EMPTY_STAT`/**S5.5** `EMPTY_MILESTONE`/`EMPTY_STREAK`/**S5.6** `DEFAULT_CODE`/**S5.7** `DEFAULT_THREAD_HOOK`/`DEFAULT_LIST_TITLE`/`DEFAULT_LIST_ITEMS`, `TemplateState` (**S5.4** `patternKind: PatternKind|null`+`patternSeed`; **S5.5** `milestoneData`/`streakData` ‚Äî shell resolves override-over-auto; **S5.6** `codeTitle`/`codeText`; **S5.7** `threadHook`/`threadCount`/`listTitle`/`listItems` ‚Äî `list` case runs `parseListItems` in `buildSpec`; **S5.8** `chartMode`+`chartPoints`/`chartFirstLabel`/`chartLastLabel`/`chartDelta`/`chartCells`), and the pure `buildSpec(id, state, kit) ‚Üí RenderSpec` dispatch (replaces the old render ternary + `BG_TEMPLATES` set). `fields.tsx` ‚Äî dumb props-driven field sections (`QuoteFields`/`StatFields`/`BannerFields`/`PfpFields`; **S5.5** `MilestoneFields`/`StreakFields` ‚Äî a status line + manual number override; **S5.6** `CodeFields` ‚Äî filename input + code textarea; **S5.7** `ThreadFields` hook+length / `ListFields` title+one-per-line textarea; **S5.8** `ChartFields` ‚Äî growth/heatmap mode toggle + reload) + the presentational `BackgroundFields`/`LibraryRail` (state+handlers stay in the shell). **S5.5** `Studio.tsx` loads `api.metrics.account()`‚Üí`latestCrossed` (milestone) and `brief.quests.streak` (streak), override beats auto, `milestoneData`/`streakData` memoized so identity doesn't churn the render effect. **S5.8** `Studio.tsx` lazy-loads both chart datasets on first `chart` view (`api.metrics.account`‚Üí`growthSeries`, `api.metrics.bestTimes`‚Üí`heatmapCells(cells,minN)`), $0 reads. `KitEditor.tsx` ‚Äî the brand-kit section (colors/handle/watermark/**S5.3 mascot toggle**/style-suffix) + **S5.4 preset dropdown / Save-as / Rename / Delete** over the `BrandKits` bundle; export/import round-trips both file shapes via `parseBrandKitsFile`. The **S5.4 background segmented control** (`gradient|dots|grid|diagonal|plus|blobs|AI image` + blobs reroll; picking a pattern clears the AI bitmap) lives inline in `Studio.tsx`, not fields.tsx. **Adding a template = 1 registry row + 1 field section**, not another shell branch. |
| `src/sidepanel/styles.css` | The panel stylesheet (~2.4k lines). **UI.8:** `:root` holds the full `--strat-*` design-token set (verbatim from `Stratus Design System/tokens/*.css`) + `--x-*` companion tokens + **legacy short aliases** (`--bg: var(--strat-bg)` ‚Ä¶) the sheet still resolves through. **Zero color literals outside `:root`** ‚Äî tinted fills use exact fill tokens (`--strat-{accent,danger,warn}-fill`, `--strat-pillar-bg`, `--strat-scrim`) or `color-mix(in srgb, var(--strat-*) N%, transparent)` (exact-equivalent, and tracks the base so Task-9 light theme flows through). Inter is `@font-face`d from `/fonts/` and set on `body` via `--strat-font-sans`; metric classes get `tabular-nums`. **UI.9:** `:root[data-theme='light']` re-tints by redefining only the base `--strat-*` tokens (aliases resolve lazily ‚Üí whole sheet flows through; `color-scheme: light`; direct-use fill tokens + band ink re-authored for a light base, dark text companions kept); density via `[data-density='compact']` and scale via `[data-scale='12'|'14']` override the new `--ui-panel-pad`/`--ui-section-gap`/`--ui-row-gap`/`--ui-root-size` vars that `body`/`.panel`/`.row` now consume. **UI.10:** `.brand`/`.brand-mark`/`.brand-word` + `.tab-group`/`.tab-group-eyebrow` (grouped rail), and a tail `.ui-*` block for the primitives (Section/EmptyState/SubTabs/SettingRow/Slider/GearPopover) ‚Äî `--strat-*` tokens only, no literals. **RL.5:** a tail `.rl-*` block (rail/detail/items/chances/testvars/preview/proposals) ‚Äî same rule, `color-mix` over `--strat-accent` for the selected rail chip; everything else leans on `.pillar-card*`/`.field`/`.row`/`.status-line`. **RL.6:** a tail `.quick-reply*` block (relative wrapper + absolutely-positioned `right:0` popover card, list rows, result/status/meta/err) ‚Äî `--strat-*` tokens only, no literals; the status line flips to `--strat-warn` via `.quick-reply-status-warn` when the clipboard refused. **GR.4:** a small `.following-*` block after the `.people-event-*` rules (`-list`/`-row`/`-handle`/`-meta` [`margin-left:auto` ‚Äî the ticks sit at the right edge]/`-mutual`) ‚Äî tokens only, and the rows lean on the existing `.person-link`/`.stage-chip`/`.status-line`/`.warn`. **A3.10:** a `.dm-*` block after the icebreaker block (`-box`/`-compose`/`-idea`/`-text`/`-foot`/`-grounding`/`-prior`/`-prior-row`/`-status`[`-sent`‚Üí`--ok`]/`-prior-text` ellipsized) ‚Äî tokens only, shape mirrors `.icebreaker-*`. |
| `public/fonts/` | Bundled Inter WOFF2s (Regular/Bold/ExtraBold) + **S5.6** JetBrains Mono WOFF2s (Regular/Bold, OFL-1.1, latin subset) ‚Äî served at `/fonts/`, loaded by the Studio (`studio/fonts.ts`, FontFace: Inter‚Üí`StudioInter`, Mono‚Üí`StudioMono`) and the panel sheet (`@font-face`, UI.8). |
| Storage keys | `chrome.storage.local`: brand kit, settings toggles (**HV.2 `passiveHarvest`** ‚Äî default ON/opt-out, absent key = enabled; read directly by content.ts AND through `sidepanel/storage.ts`'s `Settings` ‚Äî HV.3 added the key to `useSettings`'s `onChanged` filter, which HV.2 had missed, so a toggle now reaches the panel tree live), harvest cursors, **HV.3 `harvestForm`** (the whole Harvest-tab form in one blob; `harvestSendToStratus` stays separate), `replyMaster:idea(+Id)`, **AX.5 `augment:contextCollapsed`** (tweet-page context-panel collapse state), **UI.9 appearance `theme`/`density`/`uiScale`** (stamped on `<html>` by `main.tsx` as `data-theme`/`data-density`/`data-scale`; `system` resolved via `matchMedia`). `chrome.storage.session`: `radar:sightings`, `radar:dismissed`, `launch:active`, `launch:replies`, **A3.8 `manual:due`** (background-written array of due manual posts, newest-first cap 5; the Today `ManualPostCard` reads it, dismiss/mark-posted route back through the background ‚Äî single writer ¬ß7.24), **AX.6 `stratus:openPerson`** (`{handle, at}` dossier-open handoff ‚Äî background-written single writer, App.tsx consumes on mount + `onChanged` then clears via `stratus/open-person-clear`). |

## 6. MCP + integrations

- `POST /mcp` ‚Äî 21 X tools (see ¬ß3.3 `x/mcp.ts`). Client setup: `claude mcp add --transport http stratus https://<host>/mcp --header "Authorization: Bearer $STRATUS_TOKEN"`.
- `.claude/skills/stratus` ‚Äî drives the HTTP API from Claude Code (scheduling scripts `md_to_schedule.ts` with the cadence ladders 3/day `[9,13,18]`, 4/day `[8,12,16,20]`; always jitter minutes).

## 7. Patterns & conventions (name these in plans; point implementers at the exemplar file)

**Money/API discipline**
1. **One place to call X / Grok / images**: `xFetch` / `askGrok` / `generateImages`. Never raw fetch.
2. **Retire-before-snapshot** (dailyMetrics): a billed read must be unrepeatable ‚Äî take the row out of the candidate set in a committed txn BEFORE the read/write that follows. At-most-once, never double-charge.
3. **Claim-before-call** (publisher, winner re-read): commit the state flip before the irreversible external call.
4. **Refuse-before-spend**: validation ‚Üí band gate ‚Üí grounding checks ‚Üí THEN the paid call (replies.ts, icebreakers.ts, images.ts hard budget).
5. **`max_results` clamps** on every paginate wrapper (endpoints.ts pattern).
6. **costHint** when the URL can't price itself; `console.warn` on $0-priced billed calls.

**Data discipline**
7. **Deterministic event ids** `type:ref_table:ref_id` + INSERT OR IGNORE ‚Äî backfill, live hooks, and DOM ingest share one idempotent id space (people/store.ts, launch.ts). **Bounded-re-log variant (sightings.ts, NT.2 engagements.ts):** when no ref resolves, bucket the id by UTC day (`‚Ä¶:<YYYY-MM-DD>`) instead of falling back to a random uuid ‚Äî a re-scroll then collapses into one event/day/handle/kind rather than flooding the timeline. A once-ever fact (a follow) drops the date too.
8. **Best-effort side writes**: `safeLogPersonEvents`, `persistRadarDrafts`, `consumeIdeaSafe` ‚Äî a hook failure never fails the paying path.
9. **Fill-only vs overwrite upserts**: hover/launch glimpses fill-only; profile scrapes overwrite (people/store.ts).
10. **Status ratchets**: stages only auto-promote; radar drafts ready‚Üíclicked‚Üíexpired; mentions never regress implicitly.
11. **null = unknown, never "no"** (`has_media`, `pinned_tweet_id`); bucket null separately in aggregations.
12. **No derived-state tables** when a read-time regroup works (conversations C2, momentum C5).
13. **Sync SQLite**: txns take sync callbacks (`.all()/.get()/.run()`, no await inside); never bind a JS `Date` in raw `sql` (use `.getTime()`); token refresh critical section = in-process mutex.
13a. **Millisecond ties break ordering logic**: writes are sub-millisecond here, so any column an ordering/recency rule reads (`created_at` insertion order, `last_used_at` anti-repeat) must be stamped **monotonically past the row set's current max**, not from `Date.now()` alone. Exemplars both in `replyLists.ts`: items `createdAt` (RL.2), `/use` `lastUsedAt` (RL.3 ‚Äî measured: 241/500 uses shared a millisecond and 4 immediate repeats slipped through without it).
- **API checkpoint columns are never written from the page (C7 launch.ts, C10 notifications)**: `mentions`'s max tweet_id IS the since_id checkpoint, so a DOM-scraped id would skip every unseen mention ‚Äî page surfaces READ mention rows for context and route their own writes into `person_events` instead; freshness gaps close via a human-clicked capped refresh, never an auto-pull.

- **Ambient ingest = free-text discriminator + server-owned parent row + lazy prune (HV.1 `POST /harvest/passive`)**: a high-volume DOM feed reuses the existing table instead of forking one ‚Äî discriminated by a `mode` value the client-facing create route still rejects, hung off one server-found-or-created per-UTC-day run, retention pruned on the ingest path rather than by a new worker (¬ß7.12 spirit). Before opening the tap, check that **every existing reader already filters on that discriminator**. **The client half (HV.2)** is the flushSightings transport with one extra rule: the ambient flush is **warn-and-drop, never retried** (a lost sighting is a missing point on a curve, not a lost user action), its resend throttle mirrors the server's recapture window so the wire carries no row the server would only skip, and the expensive DOM read sits BEHIND the throttle check ‚Äî a scan-loop hook runs on every mutation burst, so gate order is the performance contract.

**Prompt discipline**
14. **Byte-sync prompts**: `.md` ‚Üî TS literal asserted by test; regenerate the literal when editing the .md.
15. **Variable tail**: ALL per-call content ({{TWEET_CONTEXT}}, {{PILLARS}}, relationship, guidance, idea) after the stable cacheable instruction prefix; `prompt_cache_key` set.
16. **Server-stamped fields**: `relationship`/`guidance`/gate signals are stamped server-side, never parsed from clients; persist exactly what the model saw in `contextSnapshot`.
17. **Structured outputs** via `text.format` json_schema on `/v1/responses` (`response_format` 400s there).
18. **No fabrication**: Grok may narrate only supplied FACTS; grounding blocks travel back in responses.
- **Niche persona substitution (N.3/N.4)**: `{{PERSONA}}`/`{{BELIEFS}}` (post) and `{{REPLY_PERSONA}}` (reply, single + batch) substitute IN PLACE (deliberate ¬ß7.15 deviation ‚Äî constant per niche ‚áí prefix byte-stable per niche); all niche fields are server-stamped from `loadActiveNicheSafe()` (never client-parsed) and cache keys carry `:slug:updatedAtMs` to bust on edits. The reply routes also stamp `contextSnapshot.niche={slug}` (single path only ‚Äî batch has no DB row) and load the niche AFTER the band gate. Seed-niche output is bit-for-bit identical to pre-extraction (equivalence tests in `src/test.test.ts` with independent fixtures ‚Äî never re-read the .md, it holds the tokens now). **N.5 (doctrine):** the 5 REPLY-GUIDE knobs (reply target min/max, week reply %, target band min/max √ó) are owned by `niches.doctrine`; consumers call `loadDoctrine()` (never throws, resolves over `DEFAULT_DOCTRINE`) ‚Äî `targetBand`'s new 2nd arg defaults to `{minX:2,maxX:10}` so untouched call sites/tests stay green (regression), and null doctrine = today's numbers. Doctrine is method-configuration, NOT a stat ‚Äî no gates touched (¬ß7.19). **N.6 (ownership):** `content_pillars.niche` + `channels.niche` (nullable, backfilled `builder`) make pillars/channels owned by a niche; all list/active reads scope by `ownedByNiche(activeSlug)` = `niche = active.slug OR niche IS NULL` (legacy tolerance ‚Äî identity until a 2nd niche exists), POSTs stamp the active slug, the channel `:slug` room 404s cross-niche, and `getActivePillars()` returns `[]` for a non-`builder` niche with no pillars ‚Üí the drafter refuses `409 no_pillars_for_niche` before any Grok spend (zero builder-pillar leakage into another niche's drafts). Last-active pillar 409 is now per-niche. PATCH/DELETE stay slug-addressed (admin can still edit another niche's rows). **AI.3 (prompt registry):** editable prompts live as OVERRIDE ROWS in `prompt_overrides` ‚Äî row absent = shipped default, restore = DELETE, `customized` is structural row-presence (never a diff). Call sites load `loadPromptSafe(key)` and thread the body into the builders (`buildGrokInput` opts `template?` / `BuildPostDraftOptions.template?`; a per-request `systemPromptOverride` beats the DB override ‚Äî explicit > DB > code-default); cache keys = registry sha-8 + the niche `:slug:updatedAtMs` suffix (both dimensions vary the rendered prefix). `validatePromptBody` guards edits: `required` placeholders must survive, the niche persona placeholders are `optional` (token-tolerant ‚Äî an override hardcoding its persona is sanctioned, D29d), unknown tokens warn. A new editable prompt = one `PROMPT_SPECS` entry + a call-site wire (AI.4 adds the editor routes; AI.5/AI.6 migrated the 7 existing prompts, AI.7/AI.8/AI.9 added the three new-surface prompts thread/rewrite/ideas, RL.4 appended `reply-list` ‚Äî **11 keys**). Registry defaults MUST come from PURE modules ‚Äî a route-file import cycles (AI.5's `voice/extractPrompt.ts` move exists for exactly that; digest.ts/icebreakers.ts were already pure enough). (Unnumbered ‚Äî the numbered `¬ß7.N` refs are load-bearing; don't renumber.)

**Stats discipline**
19. **Gates**: playbook cells + all lifts n‚â•20/side (`DEFAULT_MIN_CELL_N`, **HV.5**: the timeline funnel gates on its `seen` DENOMINATOR, not on measured outcomes ‚Äî `rate` null below it); angle preference ‚â•3 measured; best-times top n‚â•3; BAND recalibration ‚â•100 and manual-only. Below gate ‚Üí `sufficient:false`/null, never a confident number.

**Routing/wiring traps**
20. **Static path before `:param`** (followups+fans and rankmap before `/people/:handle`) ‚Äî check on every new people-adjacent route.
21. **Public-by-design routes** (`/healthz`, `/explorer`) mount at root outside the `/x/*` guard.
22. **LLM-gated mount vs runtime 503** (AI.6 ‚Äî was Grok-gated): user-facing-always routes mount always + check `llmConfigured()` (EITHER provider) at runtime ‚Üí 503; pure LLM routes (`replies`/`drafter`/`voiceExtract`) refuse to mount unless `llmConfigured()`. `askLLM` still enforces the RESOLVED provider's key per request (503 `llm_not_configured`) ‚Äî the mount/pre-flight gate is only "is ANY provider available". `images` stays `XAI_API_KEY`-only (Decision 6). The pre-flight 503 strings on pillars-draft/extract-winners/icebreaker stay `grok_not_configured` (stable extension matchers); only digest's degrade field renamed to `llm_not_configured`.
23. **Worker-owned statuses**: PATCH/DELETE 409 on `publishing`/`posted`. **A3.5:** `POST /posts/scheduled/:id/mark-posted` is the ONE sanctioned client status transition (`manual`‚Üí`posted`, 409 `not_manual` otherwise); it flips status only and NEVER writes `posts_published` (decision 6 ‚Äî the discovery-checkpoint trap).
23a. **Advisory, never refusal** (GR.6 `scheduleWarnings` in `calendar.ts`): a "this looks risky" check ships as a `warnings: string[]` field computed AFTER the write, inside a try/catch, so a failed advisory read degrades to no advice instead of turning a 201 into a 500. Only money/policy guards (the URL surcharge) may refuse. Same family as "a side-hook failure never fails the paying path".

**Extension**
24. **Background = single session-storage writer**; content/panel talk via messages, never write directly.
25. **One transport**: all HTTP through `ApiRequest`; blobs via `ApiRequest.binary`.
26. **Content script is an IIFE**: no module imports at runtime; shared code gets inlined ‚Äî heavy deps stay out.
27. **Shims for shared server modules** (replyBand, channelSuggest) ‚Äî never fork logic between server and page.
28. **Posting is always manual paste** ‚Äî OAuth 1.0a media wall + reply policy; nothing auto-posts to others, MCP can only create `draft` rows.
- **Design tokens (UI.8)**: the panel's `styles.css` `:root` carries the `--strat-*` token set (from `Stratus Design System/tokens/*.css`) + `--x-*` companion tokens + legacy short aliases. New UI references `--strat-*` directly; tinted fills use the exact fill tokens or `color-mix(in srgb, var(--strat-*) N%, transparent)`; **no color literal lives outside `:root`**. **UI.9** made it theme-aware: `:root[data-theme='light']` redefines only the base `--strat-*` tokens (the whole sheet re-tints via the aliases), `main.tsx` stamps `data-theme`/`data-density`/`data-scale` on `<html>` from the local `theme`/`density`/`uiScale` settings (`system` resolved via `matchMedia` + listener). Appearance is panel-local (chrome.storage), never server-synced; content-script overlays and the Studio canvas are exempt (they follow X / the brand kit). (Unnumbered ‚Äî the numbered `¬ß7.N` refs are load-bearing across CLAUDE.md/plans; don't renumber.)
- **Settings platform (UI.1)**: server-side tunable knobs live in `app_settings` (override rows) + the typed `src/x/settings/registry.ts` catalog. Discipline: **only routes/workers read the store** via the bound `getSetting`; **pure modules stay pure** and take an opts object defaulted to today's constant (`computeQuests(rows, opts = QUEST_DEFAULTS)`) ‚Äî so every existing pure test stays valid and the store is mockable. Registry floors/ceilings are the money/policy guard (an MCP agent editing via `x_update_setting` hits the same wall). The shared store (`src/settings/store.ts`) never imports `src/x/*` ‚Äî the registry is passed in. **UI.2 landed the first store consumers:** `routes/brief.ts` reads `x.doctrine.anchors3/anchors4/ladderSwitchAt` (schedule gaps + ladder pick via `pickAnchors(n, cfg)`), `x.display.sparklineDays/leaderCount`, and `x.quests.*` (through `computeQuests(inputs, opts)` + the new trailing params on `neglectedTargetsAtDayStart`/`launchesAttended`) at request time. The reply band / week-% / 2‚Äì10√ó stay **niche-owned** (`loadDoctrine`, N.5) ‚Äî D2/D30c dropped the 3 duplicate keys UI.1 had seeded, so each registry knob has exactly one owner. **UI.3 added the people/followups/pinned/digest consumers the same way:** `routes/followups.ts` reads the `followups` group per request (queue windows ‚Üí `classifyFollowups`, momentum threshold ‚Üí `momentumInflection`, reup ages ‚Üí the SQL, fan-window ‚Üí `fanUnacknowledged`); `routes/brief.ts` reads the `pinned` group ‚Üí `buildPinnedWatch(‚Ä¶, {staleDays, outperformRatio})`; `routes/digest.ts` reads its own `x.digest.neglectedCap` PLUS the `followups` group's `neglectedTargetDays`/`neglectedAllyDays` (single owner, two consumers ‚Äî the weekly list moves with the daily queue). One deliberate exception to "only routes/workers read the store": `people/store.ts::recomputePerson` reads the `people` group directly, because `computeStage` runs from every ingest path (mentions/harvest/engagements/PATCH) and a knob honored only in the route would leave the others on defaults ‚Äî recomputePerson is impure DB access, not a pure fn. The 2‚Äì10√ó band multipliers were again NOT added as keys (niche-owned, the same D2 drop). **UI.4 added the gate/radar/worker consumers + the MCP pair:** `routes/playbook.ts` reads `x.gates.minCellN` as the DEFAULT gate (the `?minN=` query param still wins per read) and the guidance loaders read it too ‚Äî a prompt is never steered by a thinner bar than the page shows; `routes/metrics.ts` and `routes/brief.ts` both read `x.gates.bestTimeMinN` (one owner, two consumers ‚Äî the best-times list and the Today cadence gaps gate identically, `annotateGaps(‚Ä¶, minN)` being the pure param); `routes/radar.ts` reads `x.radar.draftTtlH` for its lazy expiry; `workers/dailyMetrics.ts` reads the winner-re-read floor/cap at the start of each run (cap 0 short-circuits BEFORE the claim write, ¬ß7.3 intact); `index.ts::startXWorkers` reads the two cadence knobs ONCE (`appliesOn:'restart'`, decision 10). MCP `x_settings` (curated) + `x_update_setting` (write) go through the same routes, so registry ceilings hold for an agent. **UI.5 added the MONEY groups (`budgets`/`ai`/`mentions`) ‚Äî 13 groups, 41 knobs ‚Äî under one extra rule: a money knob is read at REQUEST time inside the refuse-before-spend ladder, never captured earlier.** `costTracker` takes `dailyBudgetUsd` as a number OR a getter (X passes one over `x.budgets.xSoftDailyUsd`), resolved per cost event and per `/cost` read; `images.ts` reads `x.budgets.imageDailyUsd` per call and `0` genuinely disables generation; `routes/mentions.ts` reads the refresh cap + page size before the token fetch (cap `0` refuses, and the 429 reports the CONFIGURED cap, not the constant); `workers/dailyMetrics.ts` reads the same page size per run. The `x.ai.*` knobs are the **house-default tier `askLLM` merges last** (request body > the `ai` blob from Settings ‚Üí AI > these) ‚Äî they tune the tier the blob's `null` fields already defer to, so the AI.2 settings and the registry are not two owners of one number. Threading rule for a knob whose call site also carries a caller-intent flag: give it its OWN opt (`pullMentions({pullMax})` beside `maxResults`) rather than reusing the flag ‚Äî reusing it here would have re-broken CA.1's 800-cap walk. (Unnumbered ‚Äî see the `don't renumber` note above.)
- **UI primitives (UI.10, D7 standing)**: every NEW panel surface from Wave 1 on composes `src/sidepanel/ui/` primitives (Section/EmptyState/SubTabs/SettingRow/Slider/GearPopover) + `--strat-*` tokens ‚Äî no bespoke `<h3>`/muted-`<p>`/hand-rolled controls. Primitives are pure presentation (className + tokens, no state libs, no API calls); the settings PATCH lives in `settingsClient.ts`, and the panel renders knobs from `GET /x/settings` (extension never imports the server registry). Wave-5 polish (UI.12‚Äì16) migrates the pre-masterplan tabs onto them. (Unnumbered ‚Äî see the `don't renumber` note above.)

**Process**
29. **Docs sync in the same commit**: `docs/PHASE-HISTORY.md` phase entry (NOT CLAUDE.md ‚Äî slimmed 2026-07-23; CLAUDE.md changes only when a guardrail changes), the relevant plan doc (PLAN/CIRCLES/SURFACES), the matching `docs/<tab>.md`, and THIS codemap.
30. **Smoke script per feature**: rerunnable, $0 default, `--live` for the one paid verification, cleans up after itself.
31. **No obvious comments; comments explain why** (cost trade-off, policy quirk, race). No emojis.
32. **Never write a raw control char into source ‚Äî use the escape** (RL.7): `src/x/playbook.ts` held two literal NUL bytes as a composite-key sentinel, which made `file` report it as `data` and made **every `grep` over it silently return nothing** (`grep -a` was the only way to find `classifyReplyOrigin`). Fixed to `'\0'`; identical at runtime, greppable again. One-command audit: `for f in $(git ls-files '*.ts'); do file $f | grep -q ': data' && echo $f; done`.

## 8. Cost & policy invariants (condensed ‚Äî full text in CLAUDE.md)

- URL in post text = **$0.20 vs $0.015** (13x). `createPost` guard; links go in first reply ($0.030 total). **Manual-publish exemption (A3.5, decision 5):** the calendar's URL guard is `pending`-only ‚Äî a `manual` post is pasted by hand (no API call), so it may hold a link freely; manual mode IS the sanctioned $0 link-post path. Articles likewise never hit the API, so the surcharge never applies to them.
- **Feb 2026**: programmatic replies to non-self tweets blocked on self-serve (except when @-mentioned ‚Äî unverified, `MENTION_API_REPLIES=false`). Quote-of-others blocked. Self-reply/self-quote OK (self-quote verified via `verifiedSelfQuote`).
- Token rotation: persist new refresh token BEFORE returning access token.
- Owned reads $0.001; other-user reads $0.005; third-party user lookup $0.010; post $0.015; delete $0.010.
- Media upload requires OAuth 1.0a ‚Äî **not supported**; Studio images are manual paste.
- Budgets: X soft $0.15/day (log), xAI images hard $0.50/day (429). **UI.5: both AMOUNTS are settings** (`x.budgets.xSoftDailyUsd` ‚â§ $1, `x.budgets.imageDailyUsd` ‚â§ $2, env vars seed the defaults) read per call; the CHECKS are never settings (Decision 5) ‚Äî soft always logs, the image gate always refuses, and `imageDailyUsd: 0` means "no image generation", not "use the default".
- Out of scope v1: multi-tenant, follower sync, media upload, Chrome Web Store, idempotency drafts, per-tier caps.

## 9. Tests & verification map

- `bun test` runs with `SQLITE_PATH=:memory:` (one shared in-memory DB across route suites ‚Äî seed carefully, clean up; some suites assert exact medians over shared data).
- Pure suites live next to their module (`*.test.ts`); route suites hit the Hono `app` via `app.request` over the in-memory DB; pre-DB guards in `src/app.test.ts`.
- Extension tests: bun:test on shared modules + studio (`templates.test.ts` (S5.6 code-card block; S5.7 thread-cover/list-card/parseListItems blocks; S5.8 chart growth/heatmap blocks), `chartData.test.ts` (S5.8 growthSeries + heatmapCells gate/normalization), `codeTokens.test.ts` (S5.6 tokenizer splits + `MONO_ADVANCE`), `milestones.test.ts` (S5.5 crossing logic), `brandKit.test.ts`, `mascot.test.ts`, `compose.test.ts`); DOM fixtures via happy-dom (earlyReplies); **A3.1** `src/shared/activeTimes.test.ts` (pure: normalization/alpha-mode/unparseable gate, weekday mapping + hour averaging, gridsEqual) + `extension/src/shared/activeTimes.test.ts` (happy-dom: column + flat layouts round-tripped, legend robustness, null cases); **A3.14** `sidepanel/calendarLogic.test.ts` (pure week board ‚Äî placement on local day columns, ghost slots = unclaimed anchors only + occupancy filtering, today past-hour drop, tier `hint` propagation [measured/audience/neutral, 0-intensity = neutral], overdue-manual flag, chip flags + 60-char snippet, drafts-tray newest-first, `occupiedSlotDates`, `slotDateFor` jitter [4,56]/hour; +10); `sidepanel/storage.test.ts` mocks `chrome.storage.local` for the settings round-trip + `resolveTheme` (UI.9); **RU.6** `shared/messages.test.ts` (message-guard suite ‚Äî `isRadarConfirm`; **RU.7** +`isRadarVariantsGet`/`isRadarVariantPasted`); **RU.7** `shared/variantChips.test.ts` (`variantChipPreview` truncation/whitespace/ellipsis-trim + `isReplyVariants` shape/empty/loose-angle); **AX.4** `shared/tweetContext.test.ts` (hand-built dossier JSON fixture, not happy-dom ‚Äî rich happy path exact numbers / thin person / angle gate 2-vs-3 + split-cell total / alreadyReplied hit+miss+unlinked / momentum single-point + same-day clamp / open-loop filtering + order / outcome cap).
- `extension/src/shared/notifications.test.ts` (**NT.1**): happy-dom fixtures for the notification cell ‚Äî the four kinds, aggregated/deduped/lowercased handles, the `unknown` + bad-handle skips, ro keyword fallback (apreciat/redistribuit/urmƒÉre), icon-beats-misleading-header, skeleton cell, ellipsis strip (both `‚Ä¶` and `...`), longest-block target pick, follow-with-bio ‚Üí null, non-notification element ‚Üí null. **The fixtures build their glyphs FROM the exported icon-prefix constants**, so correcting a prefix after the live browser walk needs no test edit.
- `src/x/people/{stage,engagements}.test.ts` (**NT.2**): `stage` gained a C10 block ‚Äî each engagement type is in `PERSON_EVENT_TYPES` but in neither exported stage set and alone computes `stranger` (that last assertion is what covers the unexported `NOTICED_TYPES`), 50 likes + a repost + a follow is still `stranger`, and a `mutual` history plus engagement stays `mutual`. `engagements` ‚Äî pure dedupe/id/summary/prefix-match matrices, then ingest over the shared in-memory DB: person created `source='notification'` + stage `stranger`, resolved-target vs day-bucket vs follow ids, the same batch twice ‚Üí `events: 0`, next-day re-log ‚Üí +1 (follow never repeats), invalid handle skipped, fill-only upsert, `mutual` unmoved with `lastInboundAt` untouched. **Seeded `posts_published` rows carry a January `postedAt` and no metrics snapshot** so they sit outside every window/measured aggregation other suites assert over, and cleanup runs inline + in `afterAll`. **NT.3** appended the route suite to the same file (sightings' colocation precedent ‚Äî `POST /x/people/sightings` lives in `people/sightings.test.ts`, not `routes/people.test.ts`): batch round-trip + normalized person + re-post logs nothing, invalid handle ‚Üí `skipped:1` not fatal, two follow cells with different `targetText` collapse to `processed:1` (the route's follow-null coercion), and the full validation matrix ending in "nothing was written" (every guard fires pre-DB).
- `src/openrouter/client.test.ts` (**AI.1**): pure ‚Äî an injected `fetchImpl` records the request, no network. Covers OpenAI-shape mapping (jsonSchema‚Üíresponse_format, effort 'none' omitted, `usage.include`/`provider.require_parameters` always), cost off `usage.cost` (+ $0/warn when missing), retry classification (429/503 retry via `retry-after:0`, 400 throws once), numeric-error-code coercion, and the soft budget watchdog. Cleans up its `platform='openrouter'` `cost_events` rows in `afterAll`; sets a dummy key + high budget in `beforeEach` (watchdog test uses its own low budget).
- `src/llm/{settings,ask,routes}.test.ts` (**AI.2**): `settings` ‚Äî defaults on empty DB, save/merge round-trip, garbage-row sanitize, `parseAiPatch` per-field validation. `ask` ‚Äî runtime gates, `resolveProvider` precedence, the no-silent-fallback `LlmNotConfiguredError` (both provider directions), and the openrouter dispatch via an injected `fetchImpl` (endpoint + response_format mapping + opts>settings>defaults merge). `routes` ‚Äî bare-Hono `app.request`: GET/PATCH settings, per-field 400s, 409 `provider_not_configured`, models 503. **Env-key discipline:** unset = `process.env.X = ''` (falsy, NOT `delete` ‚Äî biome `noDelete`; AI.1 pattern), saved/restored per test; all three clean up their `app_settings` `'ai'` row (+ ask cleans openrouter `cost_events`).
- Settings suites (**UI.1‚ÄìUI.5**): `src/x/settings/registry.test.ts` (validation matrix incl. the first `enum` knob, per-task group/key/scope lists, restart-scope, ceilings, and **`every registry default validates against its own def`** ‚Äî the guard for env-backed defaults) + `src/x/routes/settings.test.ts` (store round-trip). Consumer proofs live with their consumer: `routes/images.test.ts` (a PATCHed budget of `0` ‚Üí 429 with no network), `routes/mentions.test.ts` (**UI.5**, new ‚Äî cap `0` refuses before the token fetch; only pre-network paths are in reach, everything past the slot would hit the real X API), `src/test.test.ts` (`parseBatchTweets` honors a configured cap both ways, `replyLlmDefaults` moves with a PATCH). **The store is process-global across test files** ‚Äî every suite that writes an override resets it in `afterEach`/`finally` by group.
- `src/x/prompts/registry.test.ts` (**AI.3**): loadPrompt default-fallback + override-wins over the shared in-memory DB (afterEach deletes all `prompt_overrides` rows ‚Äî other suites render prompts and must see defaults), sha cache-key stability/distinctness, `validatePromptBody` matrices (missing required / optional-droppable niche placeholders / unknown-token dedup), `renderPrompt` $-safety, and the builders' `template` param (marker template renders; per-request override beats the DB template; `{{REPLY_PERSONA}}` still substitutes in a custom template; explicit default template byte-identical to omitting it).
- `src/x/routes/prompts.test.ts` (**AI.4**): bare-Hono `app.request` over the shared in-memory DB (afterEach+afterAll wipe `prompt_overrides` ‚Äî other prompt-rendering suites must see defaults) ‚Äî GET list uncustomized, GET default body, PATCH missing-placeholder 400 + `missing`, valid PATCH ‚Üí customized + `unknownPlaceholders` + `loadPrompt` reflects it + other key untouched, 32KB‚Üí413, empty/absent body 400, reset scoping, restore-defaults `{restored:n}` + list all-uncustomized, unknown-key 404 (GET/PATCH/reset), and the done-when chain (override ‚Üí `loadPrompt` reflects ‚Üí restore reverts). The bearer 401 is NOT duplicated (shared `/x` middleware, covered by app.test/mcp.test ‚Äî niche.test discipline).
- `src/x/replyLists/engine.test.ts` (**RL.1**): stubbed-rng matrices (render degradation, pick exclusion windows at n=2/3/6, humanizer step order + strict thresholds + the fixed 10-draw contract via a `counted` rng) plus seeded `mulberry32` sweeps for the statistical promises ‚Äî 200 runs asserting protected spans are never mutated and the typo rate tracks the configured chance (0 ‚Üí none, 5% ‚Üí single digits). No DB, no `Math.random`.
- `src/x/replyLists/generate.test.ts` (**RL.4**): pure ‚Äî `buildListGenInput` tail placement (request + existing items after `## Rules`), count/empty-list placeholders, a registry override body as the base + default byte-identity, `$&`/`$'`/`` $` `` survival (split/join), and the no-persona-token assertion; `parseGeneratedItems` happy path, empty/over-280/non-string drops, casing+whitespace dedupe, count cap, malformed ‚Üí null vs a legal `[]`. No DB, no network.
- `src/x/routes/replyLists.test.ts` (**RL.2**): bare-Hono `app.request` over the shared in-memory DB ‚Äî CRUD round-trip (trim/defaults, grouped counts, patch, delete‚Üí404), cascade (items gone after the list), replace-vs-append semantics (ids swapped, whole-set response, empty replace clears), item writes scoped to their list (right item + wrong list ‚Üí 404 on PATCH and DELETE), and the guard matrix (name bounds, humanizer null-clears/partial-parses/non-object-400s, item text 1..280 + the 100-cap boundary, bare-string items rejected, unknown-vs-malformed ids 404 vs 400, `empty_patch`). **RL.3** adds the `/use` describe: 10 sequential uses on a 5-item list (no back-to-back repeat, 10 `reply_list_uses` rows, `useCount` sums to 10), preview writes nothing, var fill + missing-var degradation, the use row's rendered text + normalized target, 409 on empty/all-disabled, and the guard matrix. Every text assertion runs on a list whose `humanizer` is all-zero-chance ‚Äî the route calls `Math.random` for real, and the jitter itself is the engine suite's job. **RL.4** adds the `/generate` describe ‚Äî guards only, nothing may reach an LLM: the 400 matrix (bad body/prompt/count 0¬∑31¬∑2.5/model/provider/uuid), a 404 for an unknown list *before* the call, and a both-keys-force-unset 503 `llm_not_configured` that also asserts the list stayed empty (proposal-only). Tracks every list it creates and deletes them in `afterAll` ‚Äî **`reply_list_uses` rows must be deleted explicitly** (FK-free, so they don't cascade and would leak into RL.7's `canned` attribution).
- `src/x/{playbook,routes/playbook}.test.ts` (**RL.7**): the `canned` bucket. Pure ‚Äî canned checked LAST (a posted draft that also text-matches counts `single`), a right-text/wrong-radar-target reply falls through to `canned`, empty bucket is a zero cell. Route ‚Äî the `canned attribution (RL.7)` describe seeds a published reply, snapshots `batchVsSingle` BEFORE inserting the `reply_list_uses` row, then asserts the **delta** (canned +1, unattributed ‚àí1) rather than absolutes: `reply_list_uses` is FK-free (D79i) so another suite can leave strays; the exact median is asserted only on a clean run.
- `src/x/routes/harvest.test.ts` (**HV.1**, the file's FIRST route suite ‚Äî `parseIngestRow`/`matchUnlinkedDraft` unit tests stay in `src/test.test.ts`): bare-Hono `app.request` over the shared in-memory DB ‚Äî pure `utcDayStart`, pre-DB 400s (`too_many_rows` at 101, indexed `invalid_row_tweet_id`) asserted to leave zero timeline runs behind, run created once then reused same-day, in-batch dupe + 30-min recapture ‚Üí `skippedRecent`, a row aged past the window re-captures into a 2-point series, the cap (`rowCount` forced to 1999 then **restored** ‚Äî later tests in the file would otherwise be capped), and the prune sparing a same-age `posts`-mode run. **HV.4** added a LAST describe for `GET /harvest/affinity` (+5): its rows are seeded **directly** (the 30-min recapture gate makes a multi-day history unbuildable through the ingest) under **its own run created NOW with backdated rows**, so the 60-day prune can never take them; six seeded handles cover ranking (4 days > 3 days, sightings as tiebreak), the floor, the `people`/`voice_authors` join (incl. a retired person ‚Üí `stage:null, inRoster:true`), the window (a 40-day-old author absent at `days=30`, present at `days=90`), the clamps, the 400s, and a `mode='posts'` author proving the corpus never mixes. It must stay last ‚Äî the ingest describe's first test asserts **zero** timeline runs exist. `afterAll` deletes every `mode='timeline'` run+rows plus the seeded keeper **and the seeded `people`/`voice_authors` rows** (shared in-memory DB).
- `extension/src/shared/passiveHarvest.test.ts` (**HV.2**, +8): pure ‚Äî the `/home` gate (incl. `/home/` and the `/home/lists` near-miss), resend-window boundaries, and `toPassiveIngestRow` (shape-field passthrough, `time:''`‚Üínull, 500-char clamp with pre-truncation `textLen`, missing id/handle ‚Üí null, image-only empty text still ships). Extension test files are typechecked by NEITHER tsconfig (root `include` stops at `src/`, `tsconfig.app.json` excludes `**/*.test.ts`) ‚Äî only `bun run test` runs them.
- `extension/src/shared/harvest.test.ts` (**HV.3**, +15 ‚Äî the module's first suite): pure ‚Äî `passesMinViews` (absent/0/negative/NaN floors all pass; the floor is inclusive), `parseHarvestForm` (full round-trip, non-object ‚Üí defaults, per-field fallback with the good fields surviving, digit-only numeric strings, CSV defaulting on for an older stored form), and `passiveRowsToday` (today's timeline run counted, hand-run modes and yesterday's run ignored, **UTC** boundary asserted against a just-after-UTC-midnight now, sum-not-first-match + unparseable date skipped, empty log ‚Üí 0).
- `extension/src/shared/userCell.test.ts` (**GR.2**, +11) + `harvest.test.ts` (+6): happy-dom fixtures for the `/following` list cell (plain row, badge present, a **non-English** badge that must read as follows-back and never as the name, avatar-testid gone ‚Üí profile-link fallback, a bio @mention that must NOT win the handle, uppercase ‚Üí lowercased, bio not mistaken for the name, nameless cell still yields a handle, unreadable cell ‚Üí null) plus `handleFromAvatarTestid` rejects. The URL block asserts `isFollowingPath` (trailing slash, `/followers`+`/verified_followers` rejected, reserved `/i/following` rejected) and that `harvestTargetUrl`‚Üî`isAtTarget` agree for **all three** modes.
- `src/x/routes/following.test.ts` (**GR.1**, +14): bare-Hono `app.request` over the shared in-memory DB. Pure `parseFollowingRow` matrices (handle normalization, trimmed/blank display name, the required `followsBack`, integer `listPosition`), a pre-DB validation describe that ends by asserting **zero ledger rows and `rowsSeen: 0`** (every guard fires before the txn), then ONE continuous 5-handle lifecycle whose tests deliberately depend on the state their predecessors left ‚Äî seed + in-batch dupe ‚Üí fill-only `first_seen_at` (backdated 30d first, so the assertion can't pass on a millisecond tie) with `displayName`/`listPosition` surviving a scrape that didn't report them ‚Üí empty closing batch ‚Üí 409 on a completed run ‚Üí the PATCH ratchet matrix ‚Üí **a partial run flipping nothing** ‚Üí **an empty complete run closing without `complete`** (the whole ledger survives a scrape that extracted nothing) ‚Üí the reconcile matrix in one call (`{gone:2, confirmed:1, requeued:1}`) ‚Üí a later sighting reviving a `confirmed` row with `first_seen_at` and `unfollow_marked_at` intact. Last describe covers `GET /following` (status filter, `instr` search proving `_` is literal and `%` matches nothing, limit vs total, 400s). `afterAll` deletes the fixture handles then the runs (FK order).
- **GR.6** (+6) rides in the existing route suites: `brief.test.ts` (+1) seeds a pending pair ~200 d out and asserts the brief's `monitor` block reports the `scheduleCluster` alert ‚Äî `scheduleCluster` reads **no clock**, so that assertion is deterministic where a burst/churn one would have to be baseline-relative; `calendar.test.ts` (+5) covers the advisory end to end (lone slot ‚Üí `[]`, 20-min neighbour ‚Üí the cluster line, 100%-overlap published original ‚Üí the duplicate line, a second copy of a queued text ‚Üí the already-queued line, draft ‚Üí `[]`). Its fixtures sit **90‚Äì130 days out** so no other suite's pending row can drift into the 45-min window, and both files delete their `scheduled_posts`/`posts_published` rows in `afterAll` (monitor.test.ts's `clusterCount = baseline + 1` would otherwise break).
- `src/x/monitor.test.ts` (**GR.5**, +28) + `src/x/routes/monitor.test.ts` (+8): the pure suite owns every threshold boundary (4 vs 5 originals/24h, exactly-20-min pairs staying silent, 10 vs 11 and 15 vs 16 pastes per hour, 24/25/39/40 churn marks, 44 vs 45 vs 46 min slot gaps) plus the near-duplicate arithmetic ‚Äî an 11-word text vs the same text with the last word swapped is **exactly 0.80** (9 shingles each, 8 shared of 10) and the 10-word version is 7/9, so the fixtures straddle the threshold provably rather than by hand-waved constants. **The ROUTE suite is baseline-relative, and it has to be:** every route suite shares one in-memory DB, so "no alerts on an empty DB" is unassertable ‚Äî it captures the alert set once in `beforeAll` (after its own cleanup), proves each rule by what its fixtures ADD (`count24h ‚â• 5`, the exact identical-text pair inside `evidence.pairs` ‚Äî similarity 1.0 always sorts into the listed sample, `clusterCount` = baseline + 1), and ends by deleting the fixtures and asserting the rule set came back to baseline. The `is_reply` filter is proven by a **two-step delta** (read `count24h`, insert 8 self-replies at the same instant, read again ‚Üí unchanged), never by an absolute ‚Äî another suite's fixtures can legitimately sit inside the same 24h window. Seeded own posts carry `retired: true` (NT.7 rule) and the `following` fixtures need a `following_runs` row first (`last_run_id` is notNull FK). `src/mcp.test.ts` gained an `x_monitor` `tools/call` round-trip ‚Äî it runs against the **real composed app**, so it doubles as the mount proof.
- `src/x/goals.test.ts` (**GR.7**, +24) + `src/x/routes/goals.test.ts` (+15) + 1 `x_goals` round-trip in `src/mcp.test.ts`: the pure suite owns the pacing matrix (both ratio boundaries, overdue vs achieved, the two `unknown` causes, `projectedAt`), the ratchet, the debt window (today never a miss; pre-`activeSince` days count as nothing; the `originals‚Üíoriginal` quest-key mapping proven by asserting the WRONG key reads all-missed) and the scorecard (weights sum to 100, the 3-vs-4-day gate, component drop-out + reweight). The route suite is **baseline-relative** (D103e): the counted-goal test reads the number, seeds 3 drafts, reads again and asserts +3, because other suites legitimately own posted drafts inside any baseline. Fixtures are out-of-window on purpose ‚Äî drafts ~150 d back (clear of the monitor's 3h/24h/14d, the brief's today, the digest's week) and account snapshots at **year 3000** so they win `desc(snapshotAt) limit 1` (me.test.ts idiom, deleted by exact date). The followers RATE is asserted only as "non-null and positive": `people.test.ts` leaves undated snapshots behind permanently, so which row wins "oldest inside the window" depends on file order.
- **GR.8** (+8): `src/x/quests.test.ts` (+2 ‚Äî the `originalsTarget` default/override, incl. the singular-vs-plural label) and a NEW `brief accountability blocks (GR.8)` describe in `src/x/routes/brief.test.ts` (+6). Every test in it **deletes `commitments` at its own start** rather than relying on order, and `afterAll` deletes the table plus its one seeded goal ‚Äî `goals.test.ts` blanket-deletes the same table and asserts a fresh commitment carries **zero** debt, so a leaked active row from here would break a different file. The goal fixture is `kind:'custom'` on purpose (40/100, baseline 10 d back, deadline +30 d ‚áí required 2/day vs measured 4/day ‚áí `ahead`): fully seeded arithmetic that cannot move with whatever `account_snapshots` other suites leave behind. The debt assertion is baseline-relative in the GR.5 sense ‚Äî `trackedLast7 === 3` is pure calendar arithmetic off `active_since`, while `missedLast7` is only bounded and the tier is asserted **against the count actually returned**, because the streak diary is shared.
- **GR.9** (+6): `src/x/digest.test.ts` (+3 ‚Äî the 3-vs-4-tracked-day gate, the delta present/absent pair, and one end-to-end blend proving the grade is computed from the SAME `activity.replies`/`quests` the facts carry) and `src/x/routes/digest.test.ts` (+3 ‚Äî three far-past Monday weeks seeded into `streaks`: 2025-11-03 (5 days, predecessor 2025-10-27 seeded as a cached digest carrying `scorecard.score = 60` ‚Üí asserts `delta === score ‚àí 60`), 2025-11-17 (3 days ‚Üí the whole card null), 2025-11-24 (4 days, no predecessor row ‚Üí `prevScore`/`delta` null)). **Only `questAdherence` is asserted exactly** (60 = 3 all-done of 5) ‚Äî every other component reads rows other suites legitimately own, so the score is asserted as a 0‚Äì100 number and the delta only against itself (D103e). `afterAll` deletes all 12 streak days + the seeded digest.
- `src/x/mentions.test.ts` (**CA.1**, +4): stubs `globalThis.fetch` (saved/restored in `afterAll`) with multi-page mention fixtures at 9.2e18-prefixed ids (above every other suite's fixtures, so the CAST-to-int checkpoint always resolves to its own baseline in the shared in-memory DB). Asserts a cold `getUserMentions` stays one page at 50; `maxTotal` walks 3 pages of 120 with every request's `max_results` still 50; a full `pullMentions` inserts all 120 above the checkpoint (since_id on every request, checkpoint advanced only via committed rows ‚Äî read back with order-by-CAST, never `max()` into JS, which rounds at that magnitude); caller-supplied `maxResults: 10` makes exactly one request. Fixtures omit `includes.users`, so no people rows are written; cleanup deletes its mention ids in `afterAll`.
- `src/x/routes/analytics.test.ts` (**A3.2**, +12): bare-Hono `app.request` over the shared in-memory DB ‚Äî GET `capture: null` on empty (the suite is the table's only writer; beforeAll+afterAll wipe it), the full 400 matrix (body/metric/tz/cols/rows/grid, every bad shape), a POST‚ÜíGET round-trip proving trim + [0,1] clamping, newest-wins after a second insert (same-ms `captured_at` is real under test ‚Äî the `id` desc tie-break is what the assertion rides on), and `?history=` (newest-first order, 30-cap via `count` on 1000, non-positive-int 400s, `history=1`).
- `src/x/posts/manualReconcile.test.ts` (**A3.6**, +10): pure `matchManualRows` matrix ‚Äî exact + whitespace-collapsed text equality, edited text / reply row / already-linked candidate all rejected, window edges inclusive vs just-outside rejected (both sides), two same-text manual rows over two tweets ‚Üí one link each (nearest wins), one tweet contested by two rows ‚Üí nearest row wins and the other stays unlinked, empty/whitespace inputs ‚Üí no links. No DB, no clock (fixed `T0` epoch + ms offsets). The impure `reconcileManualPosts` wrapper stays private; A3.15's `smoke-authoring3.ts` covers the link path via this matcher + a replay of the wrapper's stamp (the wrapper's own `POST /posts/reconcile` runs the paid daily pass).
- Byte-sync prompt tests (post + reply + **thread**, AI.7) fail when .md and TS literal drift.
- `src/x/routes/drafter.test.ts` (**AI.7**): bare-Hono mount of the drafter (+calendar) router ‚Äî draft-thread pre-spend guards (`invalid_tweet_count`, `invalid_provider` ‚Üí 400) and the **no-key 503** (force-unsets BOTH `XAI_API_KEY`+`OPENROUTER_API_KEY` in a `finally` so it never spends), plus `insertThreadDraft` directly (head `draft`+tails `segment` sharing a threadId, `source='drafter'`, and `GET /posts/scheduled/:id` returns 3 siblings). Thread pure tests (`parseThreadDraft`/`buildThreadDraftInput`/byte-sync) live in `src/test.test.ts`. **AI.8** added a `rewrite route guards` block here (empty/oversized text, oversized instruction, unknown provider ‚Üí 400; both-keys-unset ‚Üí 503) and `parseRewrite`/`buildRewriteInput` pure tests to `src/test.test.ts`.
- Smoke scripts (`scripts/smoke-*.ts`): ai-layer, authoring, authoring3, c6, c9, channels, conversations, explorer, followups, glance, guardrails, launch, mcp, me, mentions, niche, notifications, passive-harvest, people, pillars, pinned-watch, playbook, radar-drafts, radar-reply-flow, reply-lists, studio, targets ‚Äî rerunnable, $0 default. `glance` (AX.1) mounts the people router in-process over the REAL DB, seeds a throwaway non-retired person + one unanswered mention, asserts the glance-map entry (stage/openLoops/lastOutboundAt), then surgically deletes the rows (idempotent cleanup on entry + exit). `ai-layer` (AI.13) snapshots+restores the `app_settings` 'ai' row and ALL `prompt_overrides` rows so restore-defaults never wipes a real customization; `--live` adds ONE OpenRouter call. `radar-reply-flow` (**RU.10**) mounts the radar + replies routers over the REAL DB: `persistRadarDrafts` seeds a `radar_drafts` row with 3 variants ‚Üí `GET ?tweetId=` returns it ‚Üí `POST ‚Ä¶/confirm` (201, asserts `reply_drafts` `source='radar'`/`status='copied'`/3 variants/`contextSnapshot` shape incl. `signals.band='hot'` preserved) ‚Üí confirm again (200 idempotent, same id) ‚Üí `PATCH /replies/:id` posted with an edited variant + `postedTweetId` ‚Üí asserts `classifyReplyOrigin`‚Üí`'radar'` **by source** (empty text-match fallback map, so it proves source beats the heuristic); deletes every row on entry + exit. `--live` adds ONE 2-tweet `generate-batch` call (~$0.01) asserting 3 variants/tweet + radar_drafts persistence. `reply-lists` (**RL.8**) mounts the replyLists + playbook routers over the REAL DB: create a list (asserts `humanizer:null` = engine defaults) ‚Üí 5 templated items (insertion order preserved) ‚Üí **10 `/use` calls** asserting no immediate repeat, ‚â•3 distinct items, empty `missingVars`, no raw `{var}` left, ‚â§280 chars, and each var filled **per the item's own template** (an `itemId ‚Üí template` map, so the assertion holds whichever item the shuffle picks; the fill survives humanization because typos never touch a protected value) ‚Üí `preview:true` moves neither `use_count` nor the use rows ‚Üí empty list `409 no_enabled_items` ‚Üí `mode:'replace'` swaps the set (new ids, `source:'ai'`) ‚Üí **the Playbook `canned` delta**: snapshot `GET /x/playbook`, insert a `posts_published` reply whose text IS one use's `renderedText` + a `metrics_snapshots` row, re-GET and assert `canned.posted`/`canned.n` **+1** with `unattributed` unmoved (delta, never absolute ‚Äî the FK-free use table may hold other rows) ‚Üí DELETE the list, asserting items cascaded and all 10 use rows survived. Cleanup keys off the fixed `TARGET` tweet id + the three list names (uses are FK-free, so they need an explicit delete). Without an LLM key it also asserts `/generate` ‚Üí `503 llm_not_configured`; with one, the unknown-list **404 before any spend** (no call made). `--live` creates a throwaway list, makes ONE `/generate` call (~$0.003‚Äì$0.01) and asserts the proposal is **not persisted**.
- `smoke-studio.ts` budget step (**UI.5**): the cap is a SETTING now, so the script pins `x.budgets.imageDailyUsd` through the store instead of the env (the env only seeds the registry default, read once at import ‚Äî a runtime `process.env` write is a silent no-op). It runs against the REAL DB, so it **snapshots the operator's own override and restores it** ‚Äî from the success path AND from `fail()` via a module-level `restoreSettings` hook, since `fail()` exits and no `finally` would run (the GR.10 rule). Any future smoke that PATCHes a setting must copy this, not just delete the row.
- `smoke-me.ts` (**ME.2**): mounts the `me` router in-process over the REAL DB ‚Äî creates one entry of each kind + a followers goal + an mrr goal, exercises the `inWindow` flag (a 40-day event falls out of the 30d window, a fresh emotion stays in), asserts the mrr goal's deterministic 16% progress + the followers goal reads `null` on a snapshot-less DB, renders both context modes, then **surgically deletes exactly the rows it created (by id ‚Äî never wipes the table)**, on both success and `fail()`. $0.
- `smoke-niche.ts` (**N.9**): mounts niche/pillars/drafter/brief/voice routers in-process over the real DB; creates+activates `smoke-nutrition` (doctored doctrine) ‚Üí asserts 0 active pillars, drafter `409 no_pillars_for_niche` (no Grok spend), doctrine-driven brief quota/ratio + voice band, and a `buildGrokInput`/`buildPostDraftInput` assembly with nutrition sentinels present and ¬ß1/¬ß5 builder markers (`Alteramens`/`Naval-derived` ‚Äî NOT ¬ß6's `Pite»ôti`, D28b) absent; reactivates builder + asserts restore; **sync `cleanup()` restores builder-active + drops the smoke row on failure** (a mid-run abort must never leave a non-builder niche active). `--live` adds one `POST /x/niche/draft` wizard call (~$0.01, asserts a 3-pillar proposal parses). The live `contextSnapshot.niche.slug` proof rides a real reply-generate (D29b) ‚Äî deliberately not in the $0 default.
- `smoke-notifications.ts` (**NT.7**): mounts followups+people in-process over the REAL DB (followups first ‚Äî ¬ß7.20) and drives the C10 harvest end-to-end: one synthetic 4-engagement batch ‚Üí `{received:4, processed:4, skipped:0, events:4}`, the three id shapes asserted literally (resolved `their_like:notif:<h>:<tweetId>` via prefix match, day-bucket `their_repost:notif:<h>:<YYYY-MM-DD>`, `their_follow:notif:<h>`), fill-only proof (a pre-seeded enriched person keeps `source='mention'`+displayName while the fresh one is `source='notification'`), **identical re-POST ‚Üí `events: 0`**, both people still `stranger` with the engagements on the timeline, `/x/people/fans` showing `inboundCount:1 / engagementCount:3` for the fan while the likes-only lurker **never ranks** (decision 1, structurally), `kind:'other'` ‚Üí 400, then surgical cleanup verified by a 404. Handles are ‚â§15 chars (else `normalizePersonHandle` skips them and every assertion goes vacuous) and the seeded own post is written **`retired: true`** so an aborted run can never leave a row the daily pass would bill.
- `smoke-passive-harvest.ts` (**HV.6**): mounts harvest + playbook in-process over the REAL DB and drives the whole HV phase ‚Äî passive batch ‚Üí run (`timeline/timeline/passive`) + rows all `mode='timeline'` under the returned runId; immediate re-POST ‚Üí `skippedRecent:3`, same run (no per-POST fork); the same tweet twice in one batch ‚Üí 1 insert / 1 skip; a 101-row batch ‚Üí `400 too_many_rows` with the stored count unmoved (the guard is pre-DB); a seeded 61-day-old passive run + its row pruned by the next POST; `GET /harvest/affinity` returning the 4-distinct-day author (`avgViews`, `stage:null`, `inRoster:false`) while both one-day handles are floored by `minDays 3`; `GET /playbook` carrying `timelineFunnel` with `totalSeen ‚â• 11` and an `'unknown'` cell of ‚â•6 (the seeds deliberately carry no `tweetTime`). **Real-DB safety is the interesting part:** every row is 888-prefixed (no real snowflake starts there) and every seeded run carries an `hv6_*` handle, so cleanup's LIKE/inArray can never sweep a genuine passive run or hand harvest; today's pre-existing passive run is **kept** and its `row_count` recomputed from the survivors rather than restored from a remembered number. Cleanup is sync (bun:sqlite) and runs from `fail()` too. Reuse this shape for any smoke that writes into a table the user's live browsing also writes.
- `smoke-guardrails.ts` (**GR.10**): mounts following + monitor + goals + me + calendar + brief + digest in-process over the REAL DB and drives all three Guardrails slices, **$0**, no `--live` flag (nothing paid exists to verify). Ledger: run ‚Üí 9-row batch (in-batch dupe collapsed) ‚Üí **a partial run flips nothing** ‚Üí a SECOND run closed `done:true` reconciles (`gone`/`confirmed`/the seen-`done`‚Üí`queued` reverse edge) ‚Üí a closed run 409s. Queue: the batch is exactly the two backdated non-followers plus the requeued row, with the mutual-stage person, the `keep` pin, the 7-day grace and the follows-back row all excluded; a re-read releases **nothing** (top-up, not stack); tick `done` moves `windowUsed`/`dailyUsed` by exactly 1 and a re-tick 409s; a `keep` pin revokes a queued row on the next read. Accountability: pacing `ahead` at required 2/day vs measured 3/day, a fresh commitment reading **zero** debt, the commitment-driven quest labels in the brief, then both ratchet directions asserted **and read back from the DB** (the GET must write). Monitor + advisory: seeded burst/near-duplicate/churn and a 20-min pending pair ‚Üí the four alerts (**baseline-relative** deltas for `nearDuplicate`/`scheduleCluster`, D103e) + the cluster / queued-twin / published-twin warning lines, and `[]` on a draft. Scorecard: two far-past Monday weeks seeded into `streaks` (5 days ‚Üí a 0‚Äì100 score with `questAdherence` asserted exactly and the delta against a seeded predecessor `digests` row; 3 days ‚Üí the **whole card null**), and `factsOnly` asserted to have cached nothing. **Real-DB safety is the interesting part and differs from smoke-passive-harvest's:** namespacing alone is not enough because a complete-run reconcile is GLOBAL and a queue read releases rows, so it **snapshots and restores** every foreign `following` status (plus `commitments` and the seeded `streaks`/`digests` keys) from both the success path and `fail()`; seeded own posts are `retired: true` (NT.7); and because the burst fixtures sit inside today's window while the brief writes the C9 diary, the run **ends with one more `GET /x/brief`** so today's streak row is recomputed from clean data rather than left describing fixtures. Verified rerunnable back-to-back, leaving 0 rows.
- `smoke-authoring3.ts` (**A3.15**, closes Wave 4): mounts analytics + calendar + dms + articles in-process over the REAL DB and drives all four Authoring-3.0 surfaces, **$0 default** (every DM/article assertion sits on the pre-spend refusal ladder, so it never spends even when a Grok key is set ‚Äî the 503 line is the ONLY one gated on `!llmConfigured()`). (a) active-times POST/GET round-trip + an under-`ACTIVE_TIMES_MIN_ROWS` grid 400; (b) manual publishing ‚Äî a `manual` row created with a URL in the text (accepted), the publisher due-select (`status='pending' AND scheduled_for<=now`, **replayed read-only** ‚Äî `claimOne` isn't exported and driving `tickPublisher` needs a token) proven to skip it, `mark-posted` ‚Üí `posted` writing NO tweet id, then the reconcile linking a SECOND manual row to a synthetic `retired:true posts_published` original **via the exported pure `matchManualRows` + a replay of the wrapper's atomic two-sided stamp** (the impure `reconcileManualPosts` is private and its `POST /posts/reconcile` runs the PAID daily pass ‚Äî D127); (c) DM `POST /dms/draft` 404 `unknown_person` ‚Üí 422 `no_shared_context` (both $0, before the LLM gate) + PATCH-sent `manual_dm_logged` idempotency via a directly-inserted `dm_drafts` row; (d) articles CRUD round-trip (lean list carries `bodyChars` not `body_md`, publish stamps then published‚Üídraft keeps it, discarded-freeze 409) + the assist ladder (`invalid_mode`/`*_required`/`not_found`/`discarded_locked`, plus 503 when Grok is off). **Real-DB safety is namespace-then-delete** (D98c ‚Äî no read-that-writes here, unlike the guardrails smoke): `a315 ‚Ä¶` text / `888‚Ä¶` tweet id / `a315_*` handles / collected article+capture ids, FK-ordered cleanup on entry, exit and `fail()`; the seeded original is `retired:true` (NT.7). It does **not** re-assert the `/writer` shell (that lives in `smoke-explorer.ts`, D125b). `--live` makes ONE article assist (~$0.02) from a **Romanian** idea ‚Üí asserts English output (no `ƒÉ√¢√Æ»ô»õ≈û≈¢`) + a `cost_events` row under platform `grok` (verified 2026-07-24: English full draft, $0.0057 on grok-4.3).
- Studio (S5) browser verification (ST.9, 2026-07-18): the deterministic-render discipline (S3) ‚Äî a throwaway Bun-served harness bundles the real `compose`/`templates`/`registry` modules and renders every template onto a canvas in Chrome; confirms fonts/mascot/presets/pattern-determinism/Copy-PNG. Reusable pattern for future Studio visual QA; the harness entry is not committed.
- Gates before commit: `bun test` + `bun run typecheck` + `bun run lint`.
- Deploy: `./scripts/deploy.sh` (rsync, migrate ‚Äî aborts restart on failure, `.git-sha` stamp, `curl -f /healthz`).

## 10. Recipes ‚Äî where new things go

- **New API surface**: pure logic in `src/x/<domain>.ts` or `src/x/<domain>/` ‚Üí router in `src/x/routes/<name>.ts` ‚Üí mount in `src/x/index.ts` (mind order + Grok gating) ‚Üí route test + pure test ‚Üí smoke script ‚Üí docs sync. If MCP-worthy, add a curated tool in `src/x/mcp.ts` (in-process `app.request`) ‚Äî that bumps `src/mcp.test.ts`'s **exact** asserted tool count (now **23**) AND `docs/s2-mcp-server.md`'s three counts (total / curated tier / write tier) in the SAME commit.
- **New table/column**: `src/x/db/schema.ts` ‚Üí `bun run db:generate` ‚Üí inspect SQL for dropped seeds ‚Üí consumers. Column semantics: nullable + null=unknown when backfill is impossible.
- **New worker**: `src/x/workers/` ‚Üí register heartbeat + stop() in `startXWorkers` ‚Üí healthz staleness window. Prefer read-time computation over a new worker when $0-equivalent (¬ß7.12).
- **New extension surface**: component in `src/sidepanel/` ‚Üí wire in `App.tsx` ‚Üí API via `api.ts` ‚Üí shared pure logic in `src/shared/` or `extension/src/shared/` (bun-tested) ‚Üí `docs/<tab>-tab.md`. Content-script additions must stay IIFE-safe.
- **New prompt-affecting feature**: NEVER edit the template mid-file ‚Äî inject at the variable tail; keep byte-sync tests green; stamp what the model saw into the draft's snapshot.
- **New measurement**: pure `build*` in `src/x/playbook.ts` (gated) ‚Üí loader in `routes/playbook.ts` ‚Üí Playbook tab section ‚Üí optionally digest facts.

- 2026-07-23 `7e66a22`+GR.1 ‚Äî **GR.1** (the GR lane OPENS ‚Äî following ledger schema + ingest/ratchet routes; xhigh, no deps, **$0**; 5 files: `src/x/db/schema.ts`, migration **`0019_messy_blue_shield`**, NEW `src/x/routes/following.ts` + NEW `src/x/routes/following.test.ts`, `src/x/index.ts`). Two tables (¬ß4) + `POST /following/runs|rows`, `GET /following`, `PATCH /following/:handle` (¬ß3.4). **The design turns on one asymmetry:** a handle's PRESENCE in any scrape is ground truth, but its ABSENCE only means something if the scroll reached the end of the list ‚Äî so batches update what they see and nothing else, and only a run closed `done:true` reconciles. **Three judgement calls the plan text didn't pin (D99):** (a) a `confirmed`/`gone` row seen again is **revived to `active`** ‚Äî without it a re-followed person is invisible to the queue forever ‚Äî but `first_seen_at` is NOT reset (it is the only follow-age signal, and a bad reconcile must not erase it) and `unfollow_marked_at` is never cleared (it is churn history the 6h/24h budgets count); (b) a run that closed having seen **zero rows** gets `completed_at` but **`complete: false`**, so a broken selector can't conclude "I follow nobody" and mass-flip the ledger to `gone` ‚Äî decision 9 generalized from cancelled runs to empty ones; (c) an **empty `rows` array is legal when `done:true`**, because a scrape whose row count lands on an exact batch boundary must still be able to close its run. `first_seen_at` fill-only + don't-erase-what-you-didn't-see on `displayName`/`listPosition`; `follows_back` is notNull and **required** in the payload (a build that can't read the badge must fail loudly, not mark the whole roster as non-reciprocating). `keep` moves no status ‚Äî **GR.3's queue must filter kept rows out of the already-`queued` batch itself**. - 2026-07-23 `3a4ae56` ‚Äî **RL.7** (reply lists ‚Äî the Playbook `canned` attribution bucket; deps RL.3‚úì+RU.9‚úì, high, $0, 7 files incl. 2 test + 1 smoke, +5 tests). `ReplyOrigin` is now `'single' | 'radar' | 'canned'` and `classifyReplyOrigin` takes a **4th required param** `cannedTexts: ReadonlySet<string>` (normalized `reply_list_uses.renderedText`). **Required, not optional-with-default:** a defaulted empty set would let a future caller silently misattribute canned replies as unattributed ‚Äî the one production call site plus `scripts/smoke-radar-reply-flow.ts` were updated instead. **Precedence is the whole design:** draft link ‚Üí radar text-match ‚Üí canned. A canned use leaves NO `reply_drafts` row (Decision 6 ‚Äî polluting reply_drafts would skew the angle crosstabs), so rendered text is its ONLY evidence; checking it last means a reply that is both a posted draft and a text match counts once, as the draft, exactly like RU.9's radar rule. The loader adds one **unwindowed** select (mirrors `radarRows`; the `MAX_PUBLISHED_REPLIES` cap on the published side is what bounds the population), normalizes with the shared `normalizeReplyText`, and **skips empty strings** so a blank rendered text can't swallow a blank published reply. `buildBatchVsSingle` gains a `canned` cell built by the same `cellOf` ‚Äî counts are ungated (¬ß7.19), the medians inside the cell keep the n‚â•20 gate. Measured with a throwaway 500-use stress: with the stamp, 0 duplicate `usedAt` values and 0 immediate repeats; without it, **241/500 uses shared a millisecond and 4 immediate repeats slipped through** ‚Äî i.e. the plan's own 10-use done-when test would have been ~8%-flaky. Same trap RL.2 hit on item `createdAt`, now ¬ß7.13a. (b) item `createdAt` is stamped explicitly per row, starting past the list's current max, because a batch insert shares one `unixepoch()` millisecond and an append landing in the same ms as the previous batch would tie ‚Äî insertion order is what the panel and the AI preview render. `MAX_REPLY_LENGTH` (280) is imported from the engine, not re-declared. - 2026-07-22 `ffbdb3f` ‚Äî **RL.1** (reply lists ‚Äî pure engine: render, anti-repeat pick, humanize; dep none, **xhigh**, $0, 2 new files, +39 tests). New `src/x/replyLists/engine.ts` (+`.test.ts`) ‚Äî the whole feature's decision-making, before any table exists. **(a) `renderTemplate`** fills `{name}`/`{first_name}`/`{handle}` (name emoji/flag/ZWJ-stripped, handle `@`-stripped, first_name = first token); a var the target can't fill is removed **with exactly one adjacent separator** ‚Äî the leading `", "`/`" "` when there is one, else the trailing one ‚Äî so "Thank you, {name}!" degrades to "Thank you!" and never "Thank you, !"; a `tidy` pass collapses horizontal runs, pulls spaces off punctuation and drops a dangling trailing comma; unknown `{foo}` is intentional text, left verbatim; every unfilled var is reported in `missingVars` (never blocks the use, Decision 7). **(b) `pickItem`** ‚Äî enabled only; items whose template needs an unavailable var are deprioritized (used only when nothing else remains ‚Äî deprioritization outranks recency, so a var-free item repeats rather than blocking); then the `min(n-1, floor(n/2))` most-recently-used are excluded (`lastUsedAt` null = never used = most eligible; stable sort, input order preserved in the eligible set) and the pick is **uniform among the rest** ‚Äî pure LRU cycling is itself a detectable pattern, so randomness inside the eligible half is the point. n‚â•2 can never repeat the last-used item; n=1 repeats by necessity; n=0 ‚Üí null. Generic over `PickableItem` so RL.3 gets its row type back. **(c) `humanize`** ‚Äî independent rolls in fixed order (prefix .25 ‚Üí suffix .20 ‚Üí lowercase .15 ‚Üí drop-period .10 ‚Üí typo .05), each skipped rather than truncated when it would clear `MAX_REPLY_LENGTH` (280). **`HUMANIZE_DRAWS`=10 rng draws are taken UP FRONT, every call, whether or not a step fires** ‚Äî so a stubbed sequence maps to steps by position (0 prefix chance ¬∑ 1 prefix pick ¬∑ 2 suffix chance ¬∑ 3 suffix pick ¬∑ 4 lowercase ¬∑ 5 drop-period ¬∑ 6 typo chance ¬∑ 7 typo word ¬∑ 8 typo kind ¬∑ 9 typo position). The suffix joins with `" "` after terminal punctuation, else `", "`; drop-period leaves an ellipsis intact (`[^.]\.$`); lowercase targets the first letter of the item's own text (a `bodyStart` offset, so an applied prefix doesn't shield it) and skips a protected/`@`/`#` first word; the typo picks one of drop/swap/neighbor(QWERTY row)/double-space on a ‚â•4-letter all-letter word that is **not** a mention, hashtag, link-ish token, or inside/containing a protected value ‚Äî names and handles are never mangled (Decision 5). `applied: string[]` names what fired (`['prefix','typo:swap']`). **(d) `parseHumanizerConfig`** is the brandKit lenient parse (unknown fields ignored, bad fields fall back one by one, an explicitly empty pool honored) but returns **null ONLY when the value isn't an object** ‚Äî the one deliberate contract addition beyond the plan text, because RL.2's CRUD needs to 400 `invalid_humanizer` while still storing a partial one; `resolveHumanizer(raw)` is the `?? DEFAULT_HUMANIZER` form the RL.3 `/use` path wants. `composeReply` = render ‚Üí humanize with the target's own name/first-name/handle as protected spans. Tests: stubbed-rng matrices for all three plus seeded `mulberry32` sweeps (200 runs: protected span intact every time, typo rate 0 at chance 0 and single-digit at 5%, links/mentions never mutated). Gates: `bun run test` **1059/0** (+39), typecheck clean, changed-file lint 0-error (the emoji class had to become an **alternation** ‚Äî biome `noMisleadingCharacterClass` forbids a ZWJ inside `[...]`). **D75** (AX.7 sha reconciliation `00ec8a8`‚Üí`83f8c4d`, orphan GC'd; 3 out-of-skill commits landed after it ‚Äî `912a9cb`/`1b2a474`/`2ffca50`, all `.md`/CSV plans+evals, no source touched, ledger no drift).
